Current Affairs Commentary

The Future of Germany's Diplomatic Status 30

— Heng

Since the National Socialist Party came to power in Germany, almost all European countries have been alarmed and have been devising ways to respond. This led to the intensified unity of the French Little Entente, followed by the collaboration between France and Russia and the coordination of Italy. Most recently, there has been a rapprochement between Britain and France, and a change in Poland's direction. Looking at the changes in the European situation over the past year, France has benefited the most. However, the isolation of Germany's international status today is unprecedented. The reason for this result is mainly due to the aggressive policies of the National Socialist Party. To avoid this kind of isolated position, the key lies in changing policies. In other words, it means rejoining the League of Nations and shaking hands with other countries in reconciliation. However, observing Hitler's determination to reorganize armaments internally after announcing conscription, and his tough attitude towards foreign countries, it is clear that it is impossible for Germany to rejoin the League of Nations in the near future. Thus, Germany's isolated state will inevitably continue for a short period. However, whether Germany can avoid jeopardizing its national security due to international isolation in the long run is a question worthy of attention by those who are concerned about international affairs. Today, the international atmosphere in Europe is indeed quite tense, but very few European countries are willing to resort to war. The most obvious is that France today, although it has the greatest fear of Germany, does not have the determination to resort to war against Germany. This is because France's best interest today lies in maintaining the status quo, so that this state of temporary stability can be maintained for as long as possible. Britain, due to its position, is also unwilling to act rashly. France must take this point into consideration in order to obtain Britain's cooperation. Although the League of Nations recently passed France's application regarding Germany's rearmament, the punishment for Germany was limited to a mere piece of paper. Furthermore, France's unwillingness to commit to automatic mutual assistance conditions with Russia in the Franco-Russian accord shows that behind the scenes of European diplomacy, there is in fact a mature and prudent Britain strategizing. Since Britain and France both emphasize maintaining the status quo, their policy towards Germany naturally favors maintaining the League of Nations and waiting for Germany to rejoin. Since they want to maintain the League of Nations, the British and French sides must leave room for Germany to join, so that the door to peace will not be closed, regardless of whether Germany is willing to join. Therefore, Britain and France's attitude towards Germany today stems from the fear of harming something valuable while trying to get rid of something undesirable. Precisely because of this, although Germany's international status today is extremely isolated and the diplomatic front surrounding Germany is extremely tight, it does not pose a major threat to Germany's security.

Some may say that in 1923, when Germany failed to pay reparations, France sent troops to the Ruhr to seek compensation. In light of past examples, who knows whether France will not resort to such measures against Germany again in the future? However, in our view, this kind of observation is an overestimation. This is because the current international situation is very different from the past. First, it is clear that today's Germany will not tolerate such actions by France. Second, France's actions at that time had a considerable legal basis under the reparations clause of the Treaty of Versailles (although the British later considered it illegal). As for Germany's action to abolish Part V of the treaty this time, Germany also has a valid reason. This is because the first sentence of this part states, "In order to make possible a general limitation of the armaments of all nations, Germany undertakes strictly to observe the military, naval and air clauses which follow…" Germany's disarmament is conditional upon the general disarmament of all nations. Now that the nations are not disarming, Germany has the potential for rearmament in terms of legality. Third, Britain and France had already negotiated the points of contention regarding the abolition of Part V of the treaty, but they wanted to present it in the form of international public recognition. Fourth, since Britain and France want to strengthen the power of the League of Nations, their actions must be based on the charter of the League of Nations. Unless Germany acts recklessly and provocatively, the military sanctions clause will be difficult to implement. Fifth, today's Japan is fortunate that something is happening in Western Europe. If Britain and France act carelessly, an unprecedented world war affecting the entire globe will be unavoidable. Britain and France know this, so their actions towards Germany cannot but adopt an attitude of "not going too far." For these reasons, it would be good if Germany could rejoin the League of Nations today. If it does not rejoin the League of Nations, France, in addition to concluding various passive defense treaties with other countries, will be hard-pressed to take more aggressive actions. Therefore, in this situation, if Germany can (1) not violate the demilitarized zone of the Rhineland, (2) not take military action against Austria, and (3) not seek development in Eastern Europe, then its military rearmament will not cause war. The tough foreign policy of Germany's National Socialist Party today is probably due to a clear understanding of this kind of international relationship.

A Travel Airplane Between Japan and Manchuria Crashes into the Sea in Fog; Found on a Beach West of Oshika Island 31

Antung: According to the Japan Shipping Company's Japan-Manchuria Liaison, a Fokker passenger plane departed from Dairen on the morning of the 26th to fly to Shingishu. However, after flying over Dako Island, its whereabouts became unknown. Later, the Antung Police Station received a phone call stating that two mail packages were found one li northwest of Dako Island. The authorities believed that it had encountered difficulties due to fog and mobilized military police to search for its whereabouts. The plane had no passengers this time, with pilot Shimizu flying the plane and mechanic Haraoka accompanying him. (27th Jiji News Agency)

Antung: There is still no news about the Japan-Manchuria Liaison airplane that went missing yesterday. The mail packages carried by the plane drifted to the coast of Dako Island, so there is little doubt that the plane crashed into the sea. The sea in that area is quite windy and the search work is extremely difficult. According to a report received by the Antung Police Station at 3:00 PM on the 27th, a crashed airplane was found on a beach west of Oshika Island at 1:00 PM this afternoon. The Dako Island branch immediately dispatched personnel to the scene to provide assistance. (27th Jiji News Agency)

(Tokyo) The Ministry of Communications attaches great importance to the Japan-Manchuria Liaison airplane accident. Director Ningaoka of the Aviation Bureau and other staff are studying the cause of the accident, but have not obtained any information. (27th Jiji News Agency)

Moscow Subway to Open on May 15th 32

According to the results of the government committee's inspection, the condition of the subway is very good and it is ready to open. Page 8

Chaos in London Silver Market; Mexico Reforms Currency System; President Orders Collection of Silver Coins; Bank of Japan Also Raises to New High; All Parties Pay Attention to U.S. Actions 33

(London) The London silver market is extremely chaotic. Speculators from all over the world are vying to buy silver, but there are very few sellers. There are many transactions, so brokers spend an hour more than usual to settle the silver price. The spot price is listed at 36 25/100 pence, up 1 375/1000 pence, which is the highest price since July 8, 1922. Buyers are still not satisfied, causing the price to continue to rise by 375/1000. According to brokers, purchase orders are pouring in, almost overwhelming them. The domestic silver purchase price in the United States is equivalent to 35 625/1000 pence in British gold. The selling price in the world market has exceeded the U.S. fixed price due to the activities of speculators. Whether President Roosevelt will raise the silver price again is what speculators are currently hesitant about. According to experts, this situation is alarming, because the situation is completely artificial and can only be maintained if the United States buys heavily in the world market. Today, there are indeed Americans buying in London, but brokers cannot determine whether they are buying on behalf of the U.S. government or for speculation. (26th Reuters)

Mexico City: The government today ordered a thorough reform of the Mexican currency system. The government is also collecting all silver coins and replacing them with small-denomination banknotes. Before this order was issued, the silver price in the foreign exchange market soared. Speculators and hoarders unanimously collected Mexican currency on the market, waiting for the silver price to rise sharply before melting it into silver bars and selling it for profit. Mexican Treasury official Lopez has flown to Washington, urgently seeking to meet with U.S. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau to discuss ways to deal with the current crisis. The National Bank of Mexico announced that it will close tomorrow. President Cardenas said that he will soon amend the banking law to stipulate the exchange rate between the Mexican currency and the U.S. dollar at 3.6. The President also said that we will maintain the Mexican currency at a favorable level. The Treasury also announced that it will issue an order tomorrow, Saturday, to establish a national reserve bureau to replace the reserve functions of the Bank of Mexico, effectively making the bank a clearing bank. The order will immediately become law. (26th Central News Agency)

(Tokyo) Overseas silver prices continue to soar. The Bank of Japan's Suiyōkai raised the silver price by 3 yen, 1 kak, and 3 rin again on the 27th, setting the price per kilo of silver at 86 yen, 9 kak, 8 fun, and 1 rin. (27th Jiji Press)

(Tokyo) Due to the high price of overseas silver, the Suiyōkai announced today that it would raise the price by 3 yen, 1 kak, and 3 fun, to 86 yen, 9 kak, 8 fun, and 1 rin. The market price in the city is also selling for 2 or 3 kak and 4 fun per day, and buying for 3 kak, reaching the highest price since Taisho 9. The association also observed that the U.S. government would raise the purchase price of silver to 85 or 90 U.S. cents, and then to 2 U.S. dollars. Therefore, it is only a matter of time before the price of Japanese silver reaches 100 yen in Japanese currency. In addition, large wholesalers in Tokyo have suspended sales because they are certain that prices will rise in the future, so there is only a market price but no transactions. (27th Dentsu)

U.S. Treasury Secretary Meets with Senate Silver Faction; Future Steps Not Yet Decided 34

(Washington) Treasury Secretary Morgenthau and Senate leaders today thoroughly discussed the future steps of the silver purchase plan. Those present from the Senate side were Pittman, Wheeler, Borah, King, and Adams. The Treasury Secretary and Senate leaders discussed the following points: (1) Immediately set the Treasury's silver price at $1.29 per ounce. (2) Continue to pay bonuses for the purchase of newly mined silver. (3) Base silver purchases on world silver prices, abolishing bonuses for domestic silver. (4) Set the price of newly mined silver at $1 per ounce. It is still doubtful whether the world silver price will rise to this level. Secretary Morgenthau stated that he would consult with another leader of the congressional silver faction, McCarran, tomorrow before deciding on specific actions. It is said that this meeting will recommend abolishing the profit tax and setting the silver price at $1.29. Although the silver price paid by the Treasury has increased, the silver purchased in the week before April 19 decreased to $2,619,195, compared to the previous average of approximately $5,000,000 per week. At 4:30 PM today, just minutes before the meeting, a Treasury spokesperson stated that the Treasury had no announcement regarding silver prices today. (116th Central News Agency)

(Washington) Although foreign silver prices rose today, the Treasury Department did not raise the silver purchase price. Outsiders therefore speculate that the U.S. government intends to observe market developments before making a decision. Yesterday, the financial and economic experts hired by the government held a long meeting. As far as the general public knows, these experts have already agreed on the silver policy that the United States should adopt in the near future. Although it is impossible to know how the decision will be made, one can guess that if the experts decide to continue to implement the policy of raising silver prices, the Treasury Department would have already made an announcement today. The U.S. government currently has two options: (1) Stop buying silver, in which case there will be a strong reaction in the market. (2) Continue to buy, allowing speculators to profit. The situation of the silver problem is becoming increasingly complex due to the influence of domestic politics. Since the implementation of the silver policy has had a good effect on the United States, the silver faction will inevitably be dissatisfied if it changes course. In addition, President Roosevelt has important legislative procedures and wants to obtain the approval of a majority of members of Congress, so he is unwilling to offend the silver faction. However, conservatives will severely criticize the silver policy. Yesterday, Chinese Ambassador Shih Chao-chi met with Secretary of State Hull, informally mentioning the exchange of notes between China and the United States in October 1934 and the promises made by the United States. At that time, the United States agreed to avoid disrupting China's economic situation as much as possible while implementing the silver policy. So far, China's protest remains an isolated action, with no one responding. Mexico, on the other hand, is not unhappy to hear about the rise in silver prices, so it has not protested to the United States. For Mexico, although the rise in silver prices is sufficient to cause the adverse effect of deflation, it can be compensated by raising the exchange rate of the Mexican currency against the U.S. dollar. As for the increase in the exchange rate, it may affect Mexico's foreign trade, but the extra profits obtained after the increase in silver prices can offset the losses. (26th Havas)

(Washington) Silver Senator McCarran today advocated that the White House should immediately increase the purchase price of domestic mined silver to $1.29 per ounce, saying that this would curb foreign speculation and end the Treasury's purchases. However, the speaker said that if the silver price is not increased to form a certain ratio with gold, such as 16 to 1, then when the silver price reaches $1.29, the Treasury must absorb a large amount of silver to maintain this price. If the gold-silver ratio is 16 to 1, then the legal price of silver per ounce will be $2.18. Silver senators in general today hoped that the purchase price of domestic mined silver would be raised again today, believing that the silver price should increase from 77.57 cents to 84.4 cents based on previous procedures. However, the government has not made this announcement today. It is also difficult to predict whether there will be a price increase tomorrow. Senator King met with Treasury Secretary Morgenthau today. King told reporters that silver speculation is regrettable. There has been some speculation in the stock market recently, with hoarding. He wanted to see silver speculators take a hit. This is not difficult to do. Just temporarily stop buying or indicate that there is no reason for speculation. It is also heard that President Roosevelt and the Treasury Secretary consulted today, although the events discussed could not be confirmed, but it is generally believed that it must be related to silver. In the afternoon, President Roosevelt met with silver senators again, but the content was not detailed. Handy & Harman fixed the New York silver price today at 81 cents. Later, someone was willing to sell large bars outside the market at 79.62 cents, but no one bought at this price. It is estimated that the liquid supply of all silver in the United States is between 15 million and 30 million, while the silver bullion and scrap silver held by industrial consumers are not included. The supply of silver in the Montreaux silver market is currently less than 4 million ounces, and there are 6 million ounces still registered in the New York Commodities Exchange warehouse. (116th Reuters)

(Washington) Washington has not yet criticized Mexico's move to recall silver coins. Mexico's steps to prevent the outflow of silver were expected. Official circles in Washington are also silent on the repercussions caused by the U.S. government's silver policy. It is reported that Treasury Secretary Morgenthau will discuss everything with representatives of the Mexican government and then convene a meeting of silver senators. At the same time, newspapers still carry severe criticisms of the authorities' policies. The New York Telegram said that silver senators are elated, and some advocate immediately announcing a domestic silver price of $1.29 in order to reduce speculators, but the Treasury Department is silent. We value the Treasury Secretary, but it is doubtful whether someone with more talent than the Treasury Secretary is needed to issue a non-empty and non-absurd statement at this time. Today's policy is even more ridiculous than the purchase of gold in 1933. The authorities are simply holding a bull's tail in a china shop in their silver policy. (27th Reuters)

London Silver Prices Fall Back; Bombay Silver Prices Rise and Fall 35

(London) London silver prices fell back 1.125 pence today. The spot price is 35.125 pence, and the futures price is 35.25 pence. Speculators fear unfavorable developments in the United States later this week, so they are taking profits, which is why the market price has fallen. There were many transactions today, and brokers worked until the afternoon. There are currently two rumors in the market: one is that the United States will decide to set the silver purchase price abroad at $1.29, and the other is that President Roosevelt will only set the domestic price at $1.29, while allowing the world market price to float naturally. If so, the collapse of the current bullish position would be severely damaging. Mexico's move to recall silver coins is not surprising. This move will further reduce the available supply in the world market. (27th Reuters)

Bombay: This morning, Bombay buying prices rose 2 rupees and 14 annas to 3 rupees, but due to the loosening of silver prices in the Shanghai market, prices turned weak, falling 4 rupees to 4 rupees and 2 annas. (27th Reuters)

Increase in Outflow of British Silver: (London) In the week ending April 24, the outflow of silver from Britain increased compared to the previous week, while imports decreased sharply. Exports totaled £619,000, of which £464,000 went to the United States and £29,000 to Bombay. In the previous week, Britain exported silver worth a total of £444,000, with the United States taking £265,000. Last week, silver imports into Britain totaled £191,000, of which £91,000 came from Japan, £21,000 from Australia, and £41,000 from Egypt, a decrease of £431,000 from the previous week. Last week's net exports were valued at £428,000, compared to net revenue of £178,000 in the previous week. (26th Reuters)

Decrease in Silver Imports to the U.S.: (Washington) In the two weeks ending April 19, the United States imported silver worth a total of $2,619,000, a decrease of $1,067,000 from the previous week. Of this, $1,606,000 came from the United Kingdom, $323,000 from Mexico, $426,000 from Canada, $42,000 from Russia, $28,000 from Hong Kong, and the remainder from countries in Central and South America. (26th Reuters)

U.S. Neutrality Policy; Stimson Issues Statement 36

(Washington) Recently, the European situation has been quite tense. President Roosevelt yesterday discussed with Norman Davis, the U.S. Chief Delegate to the Disarmament Conference, the issue of the U.S. maintaining neutrality in wartime. It is generally speculated that the President may issue a declaration of a definite principle regarding neutrality. Former Secretary of State Stimson of the Hoover government issued a statement saying, "If war does break out in the world and the United States does not want to be drawn into the vortex, the only way is for the United States to cooperate effectively with other countries to prevent conflicts from occurring and thus causing a world war. As for the U.S. government formulating a neutrality policy, that is a secondary strategy." (28th Havas)

Quezon Expresses Satisfaction with the U.S. Government 37

(Washington) Philippine Senate President Quezon today predicted close cooperation between Washington authorities and Manila official circles during the autonomous period. Quezon stated his views on future cooperation to an Associated Press reporter, saying that Washington's attitude is both sympathetic and supportive. My last meeting with President Roosevelt lasted an hour and no outsiders participated. I feel that the President is very willing to help the Filipinos and has a deep understanding of the Philippine problem. Quezon also said that the Filipinos are fortunate to have President Roosevelt in power and Governor-General Murphy governing Manila when they made their requests. Both statesmen are willing to use their spirit of cooperation and exercise their powers and talents to help the Filipinos. When asked whether he agrees with the bimetallic monetary system, Quezon said that he has never considered reforming the currency system of the Philippines. It is not appropriate to discuss this issue during this transition between old and new governments. We should be very cautious about this kind of reform before taking any steps to fundamentally reform the overall situation. What is needed now is to instill the idea of economic security into the Filipinos. (26th Central News Agency)

US House of Representatives Passes $460 Million Naval Spending Bill, Largest Peacetime Naval Budget, Several Amendments Rejected 40

(Washington) The government previously submitted a naval budget proposal for this year to the House of Representatives, requesting an appropriation of $460,000,000, which is the largest peacetime naval budget. Yesterday, the House Appropriations Committee presented it for discussion, believing that the huge naval expenditure would make the American people and other countries feel uneasy. Therefore, it reduced the proposed expenditure of $9,380,000 for building 24 new ships by $15,000,000. The House met to discuss and passed the government's original proposal, and sent it to the Senate. This bill allocates a total of $460,000,000 to build 24 new warships to replace those that have reached the end of their service life, and to build 555 aircraft, and to build a metal airship with $70,000. The naval aviation expenditure increased to $52,000,000. In addition, the number of naval officers was increased by 2,677, bringing the total number of officers to 8,176. The number of soldiers was increased by 9,000, bringing the total number to 93,500. The total increase was more than 11,600 personnel. (Havas, 26th)

(Washington) The House of Representatives today resolutely passed the $465,286,261 naval appropriations bill, disregarding six amendments proposed by pacifists. This number is an increase of $174,879,098 over last year's naval expenditure. Congressman Maverick's small navy faction in the House attempted to postpone the $14,500,000 plan to build new ships, but ultimately failed. Congressman Cooper then requested that the naval construction plan be postponed until January 3, 1936, which was also rejected. Maverick told the House that the United States building new battleships might hinder world peace. However, a government spokesperson stated that the new ship construction expenses were insignificant and not worth mentioning. The bill has been submitted to the Senate, and it is rumored that there will be no resistance from the Senate. President Roosevelt has silently approved the plan to increase naval personnel. The House Appropriations Committee recently halved the new ship construction expenditure of $29,350,000, intending to demonstrate the United States' confidence that the naval conference to be convened in the second half of this year will be successful. (National News Agency, 26th)

Germany Builds Twelve Small Submarines, German Political Circles Vehemently Deny It 41

(London) News has reached London that Germany is currently building several small submarines, reportedly twelve of them, each weighing 250 tons. Whether there are other constructions is still unknown. The British government is currently in communication with its ambassador in Berlin and will consider the impact of this news on the Anglo-German naval talks scheduled for the second week of May. The Treaty of Versailles prohibits Germany from building submarines. If Germany has indeed done this, it would be another act of violating the treaty. (Reuters, 27th)

(London) According to news from Berlin today, German political circles are vehemently denying the construction of small submarines. An official from the Ministry of National Defense said that this claim is based on wild speculation and that they do not wish to comment on it. Germany currently has no submarines under construction, and there are no plans to build any, as all naval issues will be discussed at the meeting in London soon. (Reuters, 27th)

French Air Ministry Statement: Truth About Aircraft Patrolling Borders, Germany Also Issues Statement 42

(Paris) According to political circles, the French authorities' announcement that they will use aircraft to patrol the restricted areas of the northeastern border of France seems to have caused a misunderstanding. Some believe that France will force German aircraft flying over French territory to land. The French Air Ministry stated that this view is completely wrong. An official from the Air Ministry stated today that the French government does not want to shoot down aircraft during peacetime. The government's purpose in sending aircraft to patrol the borders is to identify the country to which the aircraft that cross the border belong. If necessary, legal or diplomatic procedures will be taken. (Reuters, 26th)

(Berlin) A senior official of the Ministry of Aviation today denied to the Associated Press reporter that German aircraft had crossed the French border. However, the official stated that some German training aircraft had indeed crossed the border in the past, but it was due to bad weather and entirely accidental, and they had quickly reported to the police. The official added that such border crossings are common in areas similar to the Franco-German border. Yesterday, the French authorities actually announced that, due to external reasons, they were prepared to take strict air defense measures. However, the statement issued by France this afternoon was much more moderate. (National News Agency, 27th)

Laval Announces: Purpose of Franco-Russian Agreement is to Prevent War, Not Provoke It 43

(Paris) It is expected that the Franco-Russian Mutual Assistance Treaty will be signed as soon as Soviet Russian Ambassador to France, Potemkin, receives new instructions from Moscow. At the same time, French Foreign Minister Laval declared in a speech here today that if the treaty becomes an unrestricted treaty of military mutual assistance according to the direction advocated by the French Communist Party, it will plunge the French people into war. He will never sign such a treaty. The agreement he negotiated with Moscow aims to prevent war, not to provoke it. (Reuters, 26th)

(Moscow) According to reliable sources, as a result of the four-day meeting of the People's Committee, Litvinov has issued new instructions to Soviet Russian Ambassador to France, Potemkin. According to political opinion, this move should enable the early establishment of the Franco-Russian agreement under negotiation. (National News Agency, 26th)

(Paris) Soviet Russian Ambassador to France, Potemkin, spoke with French Foreign Minister Laval for an hour last night at the French Foreign Ministry. When leaving the Foreign Ministry, the Russian ambassador told reporters that the fundamental points of the two countries' agreement had been agreed upon, but a few details had not yet been resolved, so several French legal experts will be invited to participate in the next meeting. The next meeting has been scheduled for today, and political circles generally believe that the negotiations will be completed today or tomorrow. (National News Agency, 27th)

(Paris) The Soviet People's Committee held a meeting yesterday to discuss the views adopted on the Franco-Russian agreement. This afternoon, Soviet Russian Ambassador to France, Potemkin, called on Foreign Minister Laval to present these views of the Soviet Union. In principle, the Franco-Russian agreement has already been agreed upon by France and Russia, but regarding the mutual assistance section, the Soviet Union advocates automatic assistance in the event of aggression, while France advocates mutual assistance only within the framework of the League of Nations Covenant and the Locarno Treaty. Therefore, some difficulties have arisen in drafting the final text of the Franco-Russian agreement. It is generally believed that Potemkin's visit to Laval will bring appropriate new suggestions to resolve these difficulties. Potemkin and Laval will also meet with legal experts again tomorrow. In this case, the text of the Franco-Russian agreement should be agreed upon in the near future. (Havas, 26th)

German Newspaper Criticizes MacDonald's Remarks, Accuses Him of Obscuring Facts and Hindering Peace 44

(Berlin) A semi-official political and diplomatic commentary was published today, titled "MacDonald's Lesson," which criticized MacDonald's recent article "Germany and Peace." It stated that although MacDonald's peace movement has failed for several years, he still regards himself as a European peacemaker and often criticizes Germany. Although MacDonald claims that he is not speaking for the Treaty of Versailles, his fundamental position is to maintain the situation created by the Treaty of Versailles. Before Germany announced conscription, MacDonald, in the White Paper he signed, pointed to Britain's increase in military spending as a result of Germany's actual military build-up. Now, MacDonald recognizes Germany's law of March 16 as an obstacle to peace. MacDonald also knows that future history will not completely blame Germany, but it is regrettable that he cannot clearly point out the cause of the failure. Germany's military build-up came long after the failure of MacDonald's disarmament plan. Unfortunately, MacDonald reversed the cause and effect, claiming that Germany's rearmament was the reason for forcing other countries to expand their military. His claim that Germany's military equipment is larger than other countries is even more inconsistent with the facts. Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations was the result of the complete failure of the disarmament conference and Germany's inability to obtain equality. If MacDonald obscures these facts and speaks, it will only increase the obstacles to peace and make MacDonald's hopes for Germany's cooperation in disarmament negotiations even more difficult. (National News Agency, 26th)

German Propaganda Minister Explains the Meaning of May Day 45

(Berlin) Today, all German newspapers unanimously published an article by Propaganda Minister Goebbels entitled "The Meaning of May Day," which stated that May Day in 1933 was the day the Nazi Party seized power, May Day in 1934 was the day when all physical and mental laborers in Germany united under the rule of the Party, and May Day in 1935 was the day when the freedom of the German nation and the sovereignty of the country were revived. On this day, all German people should express their gratitude for the Führer's announcement of conscription on March 16, because from now on, the unity of all German nationals will be a fact that informs the world, and there will be no more contacting others to attack their own nationals. Führer Hitler is the representative of this new national. His words are the voice of 65 million Germans. He is the spokesperson of Germany. He not only defends the honor of Germany, but also insists on the equality of the country. Finally, he will not hesitate to use all his strength and sacrifice to build peace in Europe. (National News Agency, 27th)

(Paris) The Morning Post received a report from a reporter stationed in Berlin, saying that according to well-informed sources, Führer Hitler will deliver a speech at the Tempelhof Airport on May 1, Labor National Day, "explaining German foreign policy and proposing to continue international negotiations based on the London Declaration of the British and French governments on February 3." (Havas, 27th)

(Berlin) May 1 is Germany's National Labor Day, and celebrations will be held throughout the country. Propaganda Minister Goebbels issued a notice today, which stated that "May 1, 1935, will be the anniversary of Germany's restoration of national sovereignty. The celebration of May Day this year should make the world aware that the decision of March 16 is the decision of the German people. Hitler is the mouthpiece of the entire nation, and his aspiration is to restore Germany's honor and equal rights, but he is also willing to work hard and sacrifice to build Europe." (Havas, 26th)

(Berlin) Today is the 41st birthday of Hess, Hitler's representative. Congratulatory telegrams from party departments and people of all kinds are pouring in like snowflakes, indicating that Hess is indeed one of the most popular figures in Germany today. Hess was born in Alexandria, Egypt. His father was a businessman. During the war, he served as a volunteer in the 1st Bavarian Infantry Regiment and was wounded in the Battle of Verdun in 1916. He was wounded again in Romania in 1917. After that, he was transferred to the air force. After the war, he studied history and economics at the University of Munich. Later, he was wounded again in street fighting with the Spartacus League, which occupied Munich. He joined the Nazi Party in 1921 and became a leader in this movement. (National News Agency, 26th)

(Moscow) In recent days, after a search by the police authorities, 70,000 "black workers" who do not belong to various trade unions have been arrested. Greek Restoration Issue to be Put to a Public Referendum, Deposed King Arrives in London, Denies the Matter 47

(London) Former Greek King George arrived here from Paris tonight. At the same time, according to news from Athens, the restoration of former King George is not impossible. The issue should be resolved entirely by the people. (Reuters, 26th)

Athens: Officials announced today that a referendum will be held soon to decide whether Greece will restore the monarchy. Minister of the Army Kondylis said that the Greek people can calmly decide whether they wish to continue to be citizens of the republic. At the same time, former King George, after visiting Paris, arrived in London with his guards and denied convening a secret royalist conference in Paris, but declined to comment on the Greek restoration movement. According to unofficial news, the Greek reform of the political system has nothing to do with diplomacy, so the major European powers are not concerned. Observers say that King George of England and the Greek King get along very well, so Britain will not prevent him from restoring his power. (National News Agency, 27th)

Athens: News from abroad that Greece will soon restore the monarchy has caused anxiety here. Therefore, last night, Army Chief of Staff General Kondylis issued a statement to representatives of foreign newspapers, stating that the republican system implemented on March 25, 1934, was recognized by all parties in Greece. Since then, there has been no discussion about changing the form of government. The general election for the National Assembly will be held soon. The government believes that the issue of the form of government should not become an issue of party struggle. If the votes cast by the people on the issue of the republic or the monarchy are unanimously in favor of restoration, the government will certainly implement the will of the people. If General Metaxas is determined to fight for this issue, the government will never interfere unless it endangers public safety. Furthermore, the turmoil caused by the recent riots has now subsided. The Greek people should be able to calmly consider this issue. If the majority of the people want to resolve the issue of the form of government in this way, the government is prepared to resort to a national referendum. (National News Agency, 27th)

(Paris) Although news from newspapers here stated that the deposed Greek King George participated in a secret meeting of the Greek royalists on his way from here to London, relevant parties have frankly denied this news. However, people on the King's side believe that the Greek general election on May 19 will be beneficial to the restoration of the monarchy. At the same time, people in this regard also said that if the Greek Constitutional Assembly advocates restoration, there will be no problem for the King to return to the country. Puppet Organization Abolishes Silver Dollar Standard; All Transactions Must Be in Puppet Currency; Severe Punishment for Violators 107

Changchun correspondence: The financial situation in the Northeast has recently become extremely panicked. The puppet organization has implemented a policy of prohibiting the outflow of silver dollars, but it has still not been able to reduce the degree of panic. Therefore, they have had to collude with traitors and Japanese and Korean ruffians to smuggle our silver dollars into the Northeast from within the customs. However, the degree of panic has not diminished. The puppet organization has come up with a whimsical idea, ordering the High Court and local courts to tally debt lawsuits. Most of these cases involve disputes over the price of puppet currency (i.e., inconvertible paper currency) and silver dollars. The puppet court then issued an unreasonable legal interpretation, stating that loans or sales matters of the puppet country's people should be based on the puppet currency. Even loans made before the establishment of the puppet organization, based on seven qian and two fen of silver dollars, can now be replaced with puppet currency. This is because silver dollars are the old currency system of the Northeast, which is also the current currency system of China. Silver dollars can still be used in commercial foreign trade, but silver dollars must never be used as the standard currency system within the puppet organization. The legal and financial circles have negotiated and compromised, prohibiting people from using silver dollars as the standard currency system with each other. Violators will be severely punished for disrupting financial order, and all merchants and people in various places will be notified to comply. From this, one can see the absurdity of the puppet organization and the extent of the panic due to the lack of silver. (Northeast News Agency)

Japanese and Puppet Organizations Establish Liaison and Transportation Agreement; President of South Manchuria Railway Company Has Agreed; To Be Implemented from June 1 108

Beiping correspondence: The Japanese are managing the Northeast, implementing an immigration policy on the one hand and carrying out aggressive economic encroachment on the other. The rumored Japan-Manchukuo joint transportation agreement is a key aspect of the Japanese policy towards Manchukuo. According to news from the Japanese side, Japan and the puppet organization have established a liaison and transportation agreement. The parties that concluded this agreement are the Japanese Ministry of Railways, the Korean Governor-General's Office, the Railway Bureau, Nippon Yusen, Kaiyusha, Dalian Steamship, Korean Mail Steamship, and Kitanippon Shimatani Steamship. The president of the South Manchuria Railway Company has agreed, and it has been decided that it will be implemented from June 1. The content of this new agreement is roughly as follows: (1) Issue sea and land transportation business vouchers between Japan and Manchukuo, and transportation along the way will be fully protected. (2) Establish the responsibility date for the place of shipment and determine the guarantee system. (3) Formulate new routes for sea and land transportation between Japan and Manchukuo. (4) Limit the joint transportation of goods between the main locations in Japan and Manchukuo, and create life insurance for freight merchants. The detailed measures will be submitted by the Manchukuo Legislative Yuan and are currently under review. The highest insurance premium is 900 yuan, and the lowest is several jiao per year. It is said that this agreement is planned to be expanded in the future. (25th)

County People's Corps Downsized: Liu Zuo-zhou Convenes Meeting to Further Reduce 500 Men 109

Beiping Dispatch: The bandit gang led by Lao Haozi Liu Gui-tang and others are wreaking havoc in the war zone. It was jointly decided that Liu Zuo-zhou would be responsible for organizing and commanding them, which yielded excellent results. Notorious bandit leaders such as Zhang Xi-wu and others were successively captured. This spring, with the eastern area pacified, the 1,000 newly added members of the People's Corps were reduced by 500, bringing the total number of the People's Corps to 2,000 to assist in bandit suppression. Now, Liu Zuo-zhou believes that 2,000 men is too many and places a heavy burden on the local area. On the morning of the 24th at 10:00 AM, he reconvened a meeting at the headquarters. More than ten people attended, including village corps directors Hao Zhen-shu, Li Fu-chun, First District Captain Ji Yao-xian, and Second District Captain Wu Yu-liang. Chief Liu Zuo-zhou reported on the increase of the People's Corps and stated the necessity of the current reduction. Subsequently, the village corps directors and district captains spoke one after another, discussing the matter in detail. Wang Lun Dies After Falling from Horse: Coffin Moved to Fayuan Temple, Prominent Figures Personally Attend Memorial Service 110

Beiping Dispatch: Wang Lun, Director of the First Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters and Deputy Chief of the General Staff of the Field Headquarters, suddenly fell from a horse in Zhongnanhai at 11:00 AM on the 23rd, sustaining injuries that ultimately proved fatal. He passed away at Xiehe Hospital, it is reported. Upon hearing the news, people from all sides expressed their condolences. After the body was washed and coffined yesterday morning (24th), it was immediately moved to Fayuan Temple outside Xuanwu Gate. Today (25th) marks the third day after his passing. Chairman He (Yingqin) of the Military Council and other important military and political figures personally attended the memorial service, showing immense honor. The various circumstances are recorded below:

Death from Horse Fall: Wang Lun had a routine of riding a horse for exercise every morning, circling around Zhongnanhai. On the morning of the 23rd at 8:00 AM, he was again riding along the coast of the South Sea with Hou Cheng, a senior staff officer of the Military Council, and grooms. When they reached north of Yongshun Ice Cellar, the horse Wang was riding suddenly bolted. Wang was unable to rein it in and was thrown off, his head hitting a stone projection by the roadside. The upper corner of his right eye was grazed, and he bled profusely. The groom and Hou Cheng quickly helped Wang up, but he had already lost consciousness and did not respond to calls. Hou and Wang's family members immediately transported Wang to Xiehe Hospital for treatment by car. Because the back of Wang's head was severely concussed and blood vessels ruptured, the treatment was ineffective, and he passed away at around 11:00 AM at noon.

Coffining Circumstances: After Wang's death, people from all sides deeply mourned the loss upon hearing the news. The body was moved from Xiehe Hospital to the ice room. For all funeral arrangements, Chairman He (Yingqin) of the Military Council allocated 5,000 yuan for funeral expenses and appointed Hou Cheng, Gao Sheng-yue, and aide Zhang Hong to be responsible for the arrangements. Wang's coffin was worth 1,180 yuan. The body was wrapped in silk wadding, and the burial garments were a blue Jing silk Zhongshan suit, with a matching cloth overcoat. Yesterday morning (24th) at 9:00 AM, Wang's family members went to Room 18 of Xiehe Hospital to supervise the coffining of Wang's body. Wang's wife cried bitterly on the floor during the coffining. Guo Qi-lin, Wang's old servant who had been with him for many years, was also in inconsolable tears. He Yingqin, accompanied by Shang Zhen and others, arrived at the scene at 10:30 AM to pay their respects. The coffining was completed at 12:00 PM.

Funeral Procession Route: After Wang's body was coffined, the coffin was carried out and covered with a coffin shroud in front of the main gate of Xiehe Hospital. The band of the Garrison Headquarters played mourning music by the roadside. Two companies of soldiers from the Garrison Special Service Battalion stood solemnly by the side to express their condolences. Wang's coffin was then carried by 64 pallbearers, with the band and soldiers leading the way. Chairman He (Yingqin) and other important figures walked in front of the coffin to escort it. Wang's son, Jing-Ya, carried the banner. A company of soldiers also escorted behind the coffin, followed by Wang's wife and the cars and carriages of the mourners, stretching for about a mile. The route passed through Shuaifu Garden, Wangfujing Street, Dong'anmen Street, Nanchizi, Tian'anmen Street, West Chang'an Street, Xuannei Street, Xuanwai Street, and finally to Fayuan Temple. Today (25th) marks the third day after his passing. Those from the military and political circles who attended included He Yingqin and his wife, Shang Zhen, Xu Ting-yao, Wang Shu-chang, Rong Zhen, He Jing-wu, Liu Yi-fei, Huang Jie, Guan Lin-zheng, Ji Yi-qiao, Shen Chang, Yu Jin-he, Shao Wen-kai, Cai Yuan, and approximately 200 staff members above the section chief level of the Military Council. Wang's younger brother, Liu Min (currently the director of the Fifth Army Hospital in Nanchang), after receiving the tragic news in Jiangxi, flew to Beiping this afternoon (25th) to oversee the funeral arrangements. It is scheduled to transport Wang's coffin back to his ancestral home in Ninghai, Zhejiang.

Wang's Brief Biography: Wang Lun, courtesy name Zhao-wai, was from Ninghai, Zhejiang. He was 42 years old. After graduating from the sixth class of the Baoding Military Academy, he entered the seventh class of the Army University. After graduating, he served as a captain staff officer in the Li Jinglin's army of the Zhili-Lu Joint Army, and later rose to the rank of colonel and chief of staff. In 1926, when the National Revolutionary Army launched the Northern Expedition, Wang served as the chief of the staff section of the headquarters of the National Revolutionary Army, the chief of staff of the First Army, the chief of the staff department of the headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, and the deputy director of the Third Bureau of the General Staff Headquarters. He was later promoted to director. When the Nanchang headquarters was established, Wang served as the deputy chief of staff. When He Yingqin came north to serve as acting chairman of the Military Council the year before last, Wang was again transferred to serve as deputy chief of staff. Wang's wife is Madam Zheng Zhao-yi. His eldest son, Jing-Ya, is 16 years old and is studying in the high school department of the private Yuying Middle School in Dongcheng. His second son, Jing-Ao, is still young. He has a daughter who is eight years old and is studying at the Yiwen Elementary School on Fuzhong Street. (25th)

Xie Lin and Liu Hangchen Confer: Reorganizing Sichuan Finances. Investigation of Local Banknotes Completed, Reported to Ministry of Finance for Further Arrangements 111

Chongqing Dispatch: Over the years, the various armies in Sichuan Province have collected taxes on their own, leading to a very chaotic financial situation. Since the central government clearly ordered Liu Xiang to be responsible for presiding over provincial administration, the various armies have successively handed over the power to manage civil finances. After taking office, Liu announced that from this year onwards, land taxes would be collected once a year, the original tax bureaus would be abolished, a single tax system would be implemented, and he expressed his determination to do his best to reduce the burden on the people. In the future, improvements can be expected. However, due to the exhaustion of cash in Sichuan Province, public debt banknotes and paper money filled the market. Since the start of the bandit suppression campaign, military expenditures have increased sharply, and the financial situation has become extremely difficult. Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi previously telegraphed Liu Hangchen, the Director of the Sichuan Finance Department, to Shanghai to discuss the issue of reorganizing Sichuan's finances. He also transferred Xie Lin, the Secretary-General of the Central Bank, to serve as the special commissioner of the Sichuan Provincial Finance Department, to come to Sichuan to guide the establishment of Central Bank branches and to investigate and reorganize Sichuan's finances. Xie arrived last month and immediately consulted with Special Commissioner Chen Shao-gui, Finance Director Liu Hangchen, and others. As a result, in order to discuss reorganization measures, it was decided that the first step was to accurately know the current amount of financial circulation. Therefore, it was decided that Xie would start investigating local banks and the number of banknotes issued by their reserve depots, and then report the findings to the Ministry of Finance for further arrangements. At the beginning of this month, Xie personally went to the local banks and reserve depots to investigate. Yesterday, Xie told reporters that the investigation of local banknotes had been completed and jointly reported to the Ministry of Finance by Director Liu. How to reorganize is to be decided by the ministry. The report jointly submitted to the Ministry of Finance by Xie and Liu to clarify the situation of local banknotes in Sichuan is excerpted below:

"It has been found that the Sichuan Local Bank was established in 1934. It has issued various banknotes since then. On August 1 of the same year, the Sichuan Post-Rehabilitation Supervisor's Office ordered the establishment of the Sichuan Local Bank Exchange Voucher Reserve Depot, which was managed by nine banks, including the Bank of China, Juxingcheng, Shimin, Sichuan Commercial, Chuankang Development, Pingmin, Meifeng, Sichuan Salt, and Local, specializing in the custody of the funds of several banks. The banks and the depot were independent of each other and not subordinate to each other. At that time, the Local Bank transferred the one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan banknotes issued up to July 31 of the same year, totaling 5.63 million yuan, along with a 60% cash reserve, to the reserve depot for acceptance. However, the Local Bank subsequently handled the issuance of the Chengdu banknote, in addition to the issuance of subsidiary currency notes, on its own. The vouchers issued by the reserve depot were borrowed and used in 1932, resulting in a shortage of reserves. It has now been found that as of April 9 of this year, the total number of banknotes and cash reserves issued by the bank and the reserve depot are as follows: (A) Number of banknotes issued: (1) Main currency portion: one-yuan notes: 6,800,9,347 yuan, five-yuan notes: 3,728,607.50 yuan, ten-yuan notes: 20,800,3,364 yuan. It has been found that the bank and depot have regulations for exchanging half or three-quarters of damaged and incomplete banknotes. Therefore, the five-yuan and ten-yuan notes both have odd amounts. Chengdu local notes: 60,000 yuan, totaling 31,400,1,310.50 yuan. (2) Subsidiary currency portion: two-jiao notes: 216,877.20 yuan, five-jiao notes: 1,389,906 yuan, copper coin notes (issued by Wanxian branch): 618,568 strings, each yuan calculated at 8 strings and 997 cash, equivalent to 68,740 silver dollars, totaling 1,675,525.20 yuan. The total issued is 33,076,841.70 yuan. (B) Amount of cash reserves: (1) Reserve depot balance: cash 1,722,781.78 yuan. (2) Local bank balance: silver dollars 596,450.03 yuan, half-yuan coins 84,792.48 yuan, two-jiao coins 365,359.26 yuan, silver ingots 169,781.16 yuan, totaling 1,216,383.20 yuan. (3) Chengdu branch balance: silver dollars 60,000 yuan. (4) Wanxian branch balance: copper coins, etc., equivalent to 68,740 silver dollars. The total cash reserve is 3,067,904.98 yuan, which is insufficient by 30,008,936.72 yuan. The above main and subsidiary currency notes total 33,076,841.70 yuan. Besides the cash reserves of 3,067,904.98 yuan held by the bank and depot, there is a shortage of more than 30,008,900 yuan. However, both the bank and depot also have securities issued by the Sichuan Provincial Government as a guarantee reserve. This is the situation of the number of banknotes and reserve funds issued by the Local Bank and the reserve depot. As for reorganization, it is proposed to follow the original four measures, requesting the Ministry to borrow 33 million yuan from the Central Bank to be used to recover these banknotes. 550,000 yuan will be allocated each month under the provincial funds, totaling 26.4 million yuan in four years. After repaying the principal of 23 million yuan, the remaining 3.4 million yuan will be used as interest on this loan. The remaining shortage of cash reserves of more than 7,008,000 yuan should be supervised by the Finance Department to instruct the bank and depot to find ways to convert the original guarantee reserves into cash. If there is a shortage, the Finance Department will be responsible for supplementing it. Once reorganization begins, the recovered and unissued banknotes and printing plates will be transferred together for closure, so that all local banknotes will be completely consolidated and no more will be issued in the future. As for the 10 million yuan of local banknotes originally planned to be sealed, the remaining 5,871,000 yuan is currently sealed. The banknotes owned by the Chongqing silver industry association are temporarily deposited and sealed in the treasury as a clearing fund. According to the method, the silver industry association's joint treasury issues deposit certificates for the collected funds, which are circulated for clearing, and no cash banknotes can be withdrawn. The purpose is only to temporarily control the exchange limit. Therefore, this sealed voucher should be calculated in the number of issued banknotes and should not be deducted." (April 24)

Qingdao Commerce Declines: Money Supply Extremely Tight, Real Estate Unsold, Many Large Stores Closing 112

Qingdao Dispatch: Qingdao is a land and sea port with convenient transportation. In the past, its industry and commerce were exceptionally developed, and rents were high, not inferior to Shanghai. Since last year, affected by various economic downturns, it has suddenly shown a bleak scene, and rents have gradually fallen, no longer as unusually high as before. Since this spring, the various commercial industries have declined day by day. Because they could not bear the losses, stores that closed down one after another were heard of from time to time. On both sides of the various roads, city houses, which in the past even spending thousands of yuan on commission fees could not be obtained, are now mostly vacant. The decline of the market can already be seen. Xie Feng Cotton Cloth Store, Yicheng Hardware Store, Wenxingchang Iron Store, etc., are solid and wealthy merchants in this city. Last month, due to lack of cash flow, they closed down one after another. The losses of the three merchants amounted to more than 800,000 yuan. As a result, various banks and money houses were all wary and stopped lending, resulting in extremely tight money supply in recent days. Various merchants could not operate, real estate sales stagnated, and various industries struggled to maintain, forming a sluggish phenomenon, and closures were still heard of every day. Recently, in April, those who applied to close down included Zhengxingxiang, Tiandehao, Deyuantang, Xinchenghe, Liu Chengpu, Xianjihao, Yuhesheng, Zhenhua Printing Bureau, Donghuahao, Qianjuyuan, Gonghe Wood Shop, Jinfuchang, Yitaihao, and Yongxiandongji, etc. Fourteen of them were stores with strong capital and a long history in this city. They actually closed down one after another because they could not maintain it. If this continues, without finding a way to save it, the cold market will become even more unbearable. The number of stores that applied to close down in January, February, and March of this year is listed below: eleven in January, eighty-seven in February, one hundred and forty-six in March. There are no statistics for April yet, but it is around a hundred. In total, there have been more than a hundred closures since the new year, which is enough to show the poor state of commerce in this city. (25th)

Songjiang: County Chamber of Commerce Member Assembly 113

The County Chamber of Commerce held its fourth member assembly today (27th) morning. Two hundred and sixty-eight representatives from various industries attended. Sun Shi-heng, an executive committee member dispatched by the county party headquarters, and Xu Mo-jia, a section chief commissioned by the county government, attended the meeting to provide guidance. Representatives from various organizations also participated. Chairman Cai Zhong-yu presided over the meeting. After completing the required rituals, he announced the legal convocation of the fourth member assembly. After Sun, the party committee member, and others gave speeches, the important cases were discussed. There were thirteen cases, all concerning the interests of the commercial community. Temporary motions: (1) Chairman Cai Zhong-yu resigned from the positions of standing committee member and executive committee member, which was approved. (2) Organization of a commercial arbitration office was resolved. Nine adjudicators and three alternates were elected by ballot, as well as two investigators and one alternate. The meeting adjourned after the resolutions were passed.

Suzhou: Striving for Motor Fee Reduction Resolved 114

More than ten industry associations in Suzhou, such as silk weaving, have repeatedly sent representatives to petition the provincial government and the Central Construction Committee to strive for a reduction in motor electricity fees. The progress of this matter has been recorded in this newspaper. It is now learned that the Central Construction Committee felt that the motor electricity fees set by the Suzhou Electric Company were excessive. Two new measures have been specially formulated: one is a two-part tariff system, which stipulates that for monthly electricity consumption below 250 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 6.5 fen per kilowatt-hour; above 250 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 5.5 fen per kilowatt-hour. The other is a minimum consumption system, which stipulates that the rate is 1.4 yuan per horsepower per month; for monthly electricity consumption below 150 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 6.5 fen; within 250 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 5.5 fen; within 350 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 4.5 fen; above 350 kilowatt-hours, the rate is 3.5 fen. Users can choose one of these options. The Wu County Chamber of Commerce has been instructed to notify the relevant industry associations and the Electric Company to comply. According to the above measures, the Electric Company will suffer significant losses, with an estimated annual shortfall of 150,000 yuan. Users have expressed satisfaction with the above measures. As for the reduction in lighting electricity fees, a request was also made at that time, but the instructions of the Construction Committee did not mention it, so the request for a price reduction is still being submitted to ease the burden on users.

Wujiang: Teacher Punished for Seducing and Raping Female Teacher 115

Tao Ruo-si, a teacher at the Huili Elementary School in Lili, had an affair with Wu Rui-zhen, a female teacher at the same school. In May 1930, they engaged in intercourse in the school dormitory. Later, in April 1932, Tao Ruo-si married Shen Cai-hua. Fearing exposure, Tao asked Wu to commit suicide. Wu was indignant and filed a lawsuit alleging seduction and rape, instigation of suicide, and requested the county government to handle the matter according to the law. After a court hearing, it was ruled that Tao Ruo-si, with the intention of adultery, seduced a woman under the age of twenty and was sentenced to one year of imprisonment. For the crime of instigating another person to attempt suicide, he was sentenced to three years of imprisonment. The sentences will be served concurrently for a total of three years and six months, with deprivation of civil rights for five years.

Jiading: Central Inspectors Arrive in Jiading 116

Hong Gui, an inspector from the Central Party Headquarters, arrived in Jiading from Taicang at noon on the 24th. On the same day, he was accompanied by Lu Lin-zhu and Zhou Gong-li from the county executive committee, and Pan Zhi-jiu from the supervisory committee, to inspect the Education Bureau, the Central People's Education Center, the Xuhang Cooperative Demonstration Area, etc. In the evening, he convened the staff of the county party headquarters to give instructions. On the 25th, he inspected the county government public security bureau, junior high school, etc. At 11:00 AM, he went to Nanxiang and then to Qingpu.

Conspiring to Obtain Rewards by Falsely Accusing Good People of Being Thieves 117

In the case of the theft of more than 7,000 yuan from the Jiading Bank in this city, since the incident occurred, the bank immediately offered a reward of 1,000 yuan for the arrest of the perpetrators. After multiple investigations by the Public Security Bureau, there was still no clue. A man named Hu Wan-chun outside the South Gate, who had served as a water police cabin chief, volunteered to the bank, claiming to have leads in Shanghai. He first asked to borrow 100 yuan for travel to Shanghai to handle the case. In order to urgently solve the case, the bank lent him the money in full. Hu then bought Jiang Xiao-gouzi, who was about to be released after serving a prison sentence for theft in Jiading, and instructed him to confess, instructing him to recognize someone as a tip. At the same time, he requested that the County Public Security Bureau prepare a document to dispatch police to Shanghai Zhabei to arrest a certain person, A. After being brought to the county for questioning, A claimed to be raising pigs for a living in Shanghai, and tilling twelve acres of land to make a living, and had no theft behavior. He also did not know Jiang Xiao-gouzi. Director Chen believed that Jiang Xiao-gouzi had confessed to planning the case with A, but did not participate in the implementation due to some reason. Afterwards, A would have shared dozens of yuan of the stolen money with Jiang Xiao-gouzi, so A and Jiang Xiao-gouzi should know each other. Therefore, Director Chen ordered A to stand in a crowd, and Jiang Xiao-gouzi was brought to identify him. Unexpectedly, Jiang could not point him out at all. Thus, the situation of trying to obtain rewards by falsely accusing good people of being thieves was completely exposed. Hu Wan-chun was ordered to be arrested and brought to the bureau. Hu could not cover it up. Director Chen immediately transferred the two criminals, Hu and Jiang, to the county government for handling according to the law.

Rural Areas Report Famine: Spring Relief Being Planned 118

Spring rains have continued for months, and farmland and spring crops have suffered damage, especially wheat. It is expected that the yield per acre will not exceed four or five dou. The Fourth District Office, Xixiang Township, has reported that spring famine has occurred and requested the county government to find ways to provide relief. At the county administrative meeting on the 27th, it was discussed and decided to request the Farmers Bank to release agricultural loans, and the Food Management Committee to stabilize grain reserves, and to send letters to charitable organizations to release relief rice for assistance.

Wuxi: County Magistrate Yan Resigns Due to Illness 119

Yan Shen-yu, the magistrate of this county, has been in office for more than two years. He has made remarkable achievements in local administration and various construction projects. The people of the whole county also love and respect him very much. Yan requested to resign due to illness last winter, but was persuaded to stay by the provincial authorities. He overcame his illness and continued to serve the public. Recently, Yan has suffered from insomnia. Even if he works a little too hard, he gets dizzy. As county administration is important and cannot bear the burden, he telegraphed the provincial civil affairs department yesterday, requesting permission to resign so that he can recuperate.

Public Security Bureau Cracks Down on Major Gambling Den 120

The Public Security Bureau received a tip-off last night that twenty-one members of a newly organized ruffian gang were operating a large-scale gambling den at No. 23 North Street, Tonghui Bridge, outside the North Gate, profiting by skimming off the top. Their organization was extremely tight, with sentries posted all around. The public security officers were requested to arrest them. Inspectors Ge and Qian led the police in plain clothes at around 1:00 AM, taking a detour through the West Gate. At that time, a large group of 40-50 gamblers were calling out bets, happily engrossed. Therefore, they were caught off guard. When they saw the police arrive, they fled in all directions. The police immediately took action and arrested twenty men and women, including the gamblers Chen Jin-si, Tang Ji-sheng, and Xu Liu-shi, along with the gambling equipment and gambling money of 177 yuan. They were all taken to the bureau for interrogation and detention. Yesterday, the gambling boss, Chen Ren-quan, and the homeowner, Guo, also turned themselves in. They were immediately sent to the court for trial together. At the same time, the Public Security Bureau issued four seals and sealed up the gambling den.

Six Steamship Companies' Competing Navigation Dispute Resolved 121

Recently, the County Construction Bureau learned that the Tongda Steamship Company, the Limin Steamship, the Hongsheng Steamship Company Hongsheng, the Xinan Steamship Company Huifeng, the Datong Steamship Company Xilu Class, were competing for business, arbitrarily changing the sailing times, and reducing ticket prices, vying to solicit passengers and overcrowding the ships. Not only were passengers unable to keep track of the schedules, but it was also easy for accidents to occur and it caused the Northeast and Xinjie two steamship companies to repeatedly requested correction, but they were not followed. Yesterday, in order to mediate the dispute, the Construction Bureau specially invited representatives of the above six steamship companies, including Chen Xiang-chun, to the bureau for a meeting. It was decided that: (1) The sailing times, passenger capacity, and stopping points along the way for each steamship must be strictly in accordance with the schedule attached to the applied for navigation license from today onwards, and no changes are allowed. (2) Ticket prices for each section should be fairly determined by each steamship company according to the mileage, and displayed to passengers. The Construction Bureau should be notified for record, and no arbitrary increases or decreases are allowed after verification. (3) Calling and soliciting passengers by each steamship company is absolutely prohibited.

Jiangyin: Northern Section of Canal Project Nearing Completion 122

The dredging of the Huangtian Port South Canal project, from the port to the South Gate section, will be completed in a few days. The section from South Gate to Qingyang is still under construction. Now, because seedling transplanting is approaching and farmers will soon be busy, the canal project should be completed quickly to avoid affecting agricultural activities. It has now been decided to first complete the clearance of the northern section and then open the dam. Yesterday (26th), Xiao Kai-ying, the chief secretary of the Construction Department, and Chen Zhi-ding, the director of the general engineering office, came to Cheng. In the afternoon, they inspected the project around the port outside the North Gate with County Magistrate and Chen Bing-zhang from the three departments and others. They immediately instructed to speed up the work. It is heard that after the completion of the project, Director Shen of the Construction Department will personally come to Cheng for acceptance.

Nantong: Case of County Police Captain's Dereliction of Duty 123

Yan Dian-nan, the captain of the Nantong County Police Force, lost more than a hundred firearms while suppressing bandits in the eastern countryside and harassed the people. He was dismissed from his position and investigated by the province. This case was designated for trial by the Wu County Local Court. Because there were as many as fifty victims and witnesses in the case, the Nantong Court was specifically entrusted to summon one thousand people and witnesses in the case near them on the 27th.

Jiaxing Municipal School Teachers' Strike 124

The Jiaxing education funds have been in arrears for more than nine months. Recently, with the approval of the province, provincial public bonds of 27,800 yuan were designated as educational savings. The county has now received them from the province. At that time, the principals of each school requested that the public bonds be used to pay off old debts, and the county government agreed. Recently, the county government stated that education funds could not be collected and planned to use the public bonds to offset the April expenses. The old debts were refused, causing all teachers on the 26th, together with the principals, to submit a general resignation and implement a strike. The principals were also unable to cope and allowed the students to self-study in the classrooms. At the same time, they telegraphed the provincial government's education department and the county party headquarters to request relief, and issued a declaration seeking assistance from all sectors. The students of each school were also concerned about their studies (especially the graduating students of all levels who were anxious). That afternoon, they went to the county government to petition for transfer certificates. On the 27th, the students of each school went to school as usual. The teachers, at a meeting at the commercial school on the evening of the 26th, after the head of the education section, Shen Da, and the principals tried their best to retain them, agreed to temporarily take on the responsibility of managing the children, but still stopped classes and waited for a resolution. The parents of the students, seeing this, were about to question the education authorities. After County Magistrate Wang returned to the county from the province on the 27th, he only agreed to use the public bonds to pay off old debts and refused to issue any more, resulting in a stalemate and escalating the situation. The district primary schools also went on strike on the afternoon of the 27th due to the arrears of seven months of funding.

Hangzhou Collapsing Wall Injures Six Children 125

A large silk shop at No. 36 Baoyoufang in Hangzhou City was destroyed by fire at the beginning of last month. A fire wall remained at the site, but has not been demolished. Yesterday at 3:35 PM, six scavenging children were picking up debris there when the wall suddenly collapsed, and all six children were buried. They were rescued from the pile of mud, all with head wounds and bleeding. The Public Security Bureau sent an ambulance to take the injured to the Municipal Hospital for treatment.
