Local News

### The Central Bank's Directors, Supervisors, President, and Vice Presidents Take Oath of Office Yesterday Wu Tiecheng Represented the Central Party Headquarters, and Chu Minyi Represented the National Government to Supervise the Oath-Taking Ceremony. Guest Lu Xuepu Delivered a Congratulatory Speech, and Kong Xiangxi Delivered a Reply Speech. 126

The directors, supervisors, president, and vice presidents of the Central Bank held an oath-taking ceremony at 10:00 AM yesterday on the third floor of the bank. Wu Tiecheng of the Central Party Headquarters and Chu Minyi of the National Government were sent to supervise the oath-taking ceremony. After the ceremony, the first meeting of the directors and supervisors was held immediately. At 11:00 AM, President Kong hosted a banquet at the Central Bank to celebrate with the directors and supervisors. The details are as follows:

Order of the Ceremony: (1) All stand at attention; (2) Bow three times to the Party and National Flag and the portrait of Sun Yat-sen; (3) The chairman respectfully reads Sun Yat-sen's will; (4) Three minutes of silence; (5) Oath-taking; (6) The representative of the Central Party Headquarters delivers an instruction speech; (7) The representative of the National Government delivers an instruction speech; (8) Guests deliver speeches; (9) The president and vice presidents deliver reply speeches; (10) Ceremony concludes with a group photo.

List of Guests: In addition to all the directors and supervisors of the Central Bank, those who participated in the ceremony yesterday morning included Central representatives Wu Tiecheng, National Government representative Chu Minyi, and guests from all walks of life including Lu Xuepu, Xie Yi, Wang Yansong, Xu Xinliu, Du Yuesheng, Chen Zhaqing, Baker, Guo Bingwen, Yu Zuoting, Liang Shuming, Li Fusun, Dai Mingli, Jiang Lufu, and key staff members of the bank, totaling more than 100 people.

List of Directors and Supervisors: The directors of the Central Bank are Kong Xiangxi, Song Ziwen, Ye Chucang, Zhang Jiaao, Chen Hang, Ye Yu, Wang Baolun, Tang Shoumin, Qian Yongming, Chen Huide, Rong Zongjing, Zhou Zongliang, Tang Youren, Xu Kan, and Song Ziliang, totaling fifteen people. The supervisors are Li Ming, Yu Hede, Bei Zuyi, Lin Kanghou, Xu Chenmian, Xie Mingxun, and Qin Zuze, totaling seven people.

Original Text of the Oath: All the directors, supervisors, president, and vice presidents stood solemnly in front of the podium, each raised their right hand to read the oath. The oath read: "I solemnly swear that I will恪遵 Sun Yat-sen's will, obey the Party's principles, abide by national laws and regulations, be loyal and diligent in my duties, save expenses, never hire useless personnel, never engage in private fraud, and never accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment from the Party."

Wu's Speech: Wu Tiecheng, the representative of the Central Executive Committee, delivered an instruction speech, saying, "Today, the president, directors, and supervisors of the Central Bank are taking the oath of office. I am very honored to be appointed to participate in the ceremony. The Central Bank is a national bank, and it is also the highest authority in the country's financial system. Under the leadership of former President Song and President Kong, and all the directors and supervisors, the foundation of the national bank has been firmly established, and its credit has been remarkable. This is a fortunate thing for our country's finance. This time, many directors and supervisors have been added, all of whom are responsible leaders in society, undoubtedly adding fresh troops. Its future development can be predicted. I sincerely wish the Central Bank a boundless future."

Chu's Speech: Chu Minyi, the representative of the National Government and the Executive Yuan, then delivered an instruction speech, saying, "Shanghai is the hub of China's industry and commerce, so the government specially established the Central Bank here. Since its establishment, it has been carefully managed by former President Song and President Kong, and to this day, it has established the status of a national bank. All its businesses are thriving and are not inferior to the national banks of Eastern and Western countries. Today, President Kong, Vice Presidents Zhang and Chen, and all the directors and supervisors are taking office by order, and I am extremely honored to be ordered by the National Government and the Executive Yuan to supervise the oath-taking ceremony. I believe that in recent years, our country's agricultural production has declined, and industry has withered, resulting in a lack of improvement in various trades. Imports have reached an alarming amount. Recently, the outflow of silver has become even more serious. In the face of the domestic and international economic situation, our national bank must respond to the needs of the times and take appropriate paths. All of you are either financial experts or banking giants. In this environment, I hope that you can work together, proceed steadily, restore the stability of the country's finances, and provide a basis for all industries and businesses to achieve the expectation of completing the task of the national bank. This is what I want to say to you in addition to my congratulations."

Guest's Congratulatory Speech: Guest Lu Xuepu delivered a short congratulatory speech, saying, "The Central Bank is the bank of banks. Since the silver issue has become increasingly serious, the Central, China, and Communications Banks have worked together to make efforts, and its success can be predicted. Today, the president, directors, and supervisors of the Central Bank are taking office, and I am here to congratulate them. I wish the Central Bank ten thousand years, the three presidents and vice presidents Kong, Zhang, and Chen ten thousand years, and all the directors and supervisors ten thousand years."

Kong's Reply Speech: After the representatives of the Central Party Headquarters and the National Government delivered their speeches, President Kong replied on behalf of all the directors and supervisors, saying, "Today, all the directors, supervisors, president, and vice presidents are taking office by order and holding an oath-taking ceremony. We are honored to have Mayor Wu specially sent by the Central Party Headquarters, Secretary-General Chu specially sent by the National Government, and guest Lu Xuepu and others deliver speeches. I would like to express my gratitude on behalf of all the directors and supervisors. The establishment of the Central Bank is based on Sun Yat-sen's teachings. When Sun Yat-sen was in Guangdong, he organized the Central Bank for the convenience of revenue and expenditure and economic construction. The former president, Mr. Song Ziwen, worked hard in the midst of storms, so the Central Bank has achieved its current results. Mr. Song's contribution is great. Recently, in order to consolidate the financial sector and revive industry and commerce, the Central, China, and Communications Banks have implemented cooperation, which is a cause for celebration. I have limited knowledge, so in addition to one vice president, I have added another vice president, Mr. Zhang Gongquan, to take the post. Mr. Zhang has a glorious history and experience in the financial sector, so the Central Bank will become more and more developed in the future. The consolidation of social finance and the revival of industry and commerce will also advance with it."

Joint Meeting of Directors and Supervisors: The oath-taking ceremony concluded after half an hour. All the representatives and guests stepped forward to shake hands with President Kong, Vice Presidents Zhang and Chen, and all the directors and supervisors to congratulate them. Then, the first joint meeting of directors and supervisors after the increase in capital was held in the directors' room, chaired by President Kong Xiangxi. The ceremony was performed as usual. The new and old directors and supervisors were immediately introduced, and the bank's business after the capital increase was reported. No motions were submitted for discussion. After the meeting, a banquet was held in the auditorium to celebrate.

Group photo after the inauguration of the Central Bank's president, vice presidents, directors, and supervisors (photographed by Qichang)

The American Economic Survey Mission Held an Expert Meeting with the Chinese Side Yesterday Was Invited to a Tea Party by Finance Minister Kong The Reception Office Will Also Hold a Tea Party Today 127

According to the Central News Agency, the American Economic Survey Mission held an expert meeting with Chinese leaders from all walks of life yesterday afternoon to discuss Sino-American commercial issues. The head of the delegation, Forbes, participated in the Pacific United Conference. In the afternoon, he went to Finance Minister Kong's grand tea party. More than 300 Chinese and foreign guests attended. This afternoon, the head of the reception office, Zhang Jia'ao, and all the executive committee members hosted a tea party at the Huxi Villa on Hongqiao Road. The Central News Agency reporter specially reported the details as follows:

Expert Meeting Held by Both Sides

Yesterday at 12:30 PM, members of the survey mission and Chinese leaders from all walks of life held an expert meeting and had lunch on the second floor of the International Hotel. The Chinese experts who attended included Xu Xinliu, Liu Dajun, Chen Liting, Zhang Naiqi, Gu Jiga, Jin Luqin, Nie Lusheng, Li Zufan, Li Zufa, Zhang Xiaomei, Guo Bingwen, Shao Huihua, Cai Wuji, Kong Shie, He Dequan, and Pan Guangjiong. Xu Xinliu, director of the motion group, was elected as chairman. The members of the survey mission included Carroll, Dilingham, Connick, Rogers, Raymer, Shifley, Hutchins, Speth, and Wexby. More than 30 people from both sides jointly discussed various commercial and economic issues between China and the United States. The members of each delegation expressed their opinions in order to reach a common understanding on each issue and then use this as a starting point for discussion. The discussion lasted for two hours. The head of the delegation, Forbes, did not attend because he went to the Capital Hotel to participate in the Pacific Federation Conference. He was represented by the deputy head of the delegation, Carroll.

Welcome Reception by the Pacific Federation Conference

At the same time, the Pacific Federation Conference in Shanghai held a meeting at the Capital Hotel on Fuzhou Road and invited Forbes to lunch. During the meeting, Kong Xiangxi, the president of the conference, gave a speech introducing the importance of the American Economic Survey Mission's mission, which is not only to develop trade between China and the United States, but also to have a great relationship with merchants from various countries in Shanghai. As far as Mr. Forbes himself is concerned, he is a diplomat, banker, and philosopher. After Kong finished the introduction, Forbes stood up and gave a speech, which is as follows: "According to my experience over the years, I deeply feel that the Pacific coast will become the largest market in the world. Looking at the Asian coast, there are China, Japan, the Dutch East Indies, and India, which have a large population. On the east coast, there is the United States, which has a vast territory, abundant resources, and a sparse population. In addition, the people of that country are developing natural resources and working hard in commerce, so the trade of the Pacific countries will definitely be comparable to the Atlantic Ocean in the future. Looking at it historically, a large population is enough to increase trade. This is an inevitable example. Now that the population on both sides of the Pacific Ocean is increasing day by day, its commerce will undoubtedly become more and more developed. If we want to study the commerce between China and the United States, we can only calculate the trade between the United States and other places, such as the Philippines, Japan, and Honolulu, as a percentage, and then compare it with the population of China. Then we believe that the trade between China and the United States must have a very large development potential. I mentioned today that the progress of transportation in the Pacific Ocean, in addition to agile steamships, also includes telephones, wireless telegraphs, and airplanes, which are enough to make the two sides of the Pacific Ocean closer and generate more and more beneficial trade. The purpose of our delegation is to make historical and factual investigations into the causes of commercial prosperity and decline, study its origins, and finally compile a report based on existing principles to develop commerce, reduce its obstacles, and make suggestions for new businesses. We will start compiling the report on the way back. Before the report is compiled, it is difficult to express any opinions. What is most noteworthy about our visit is the internal transportation in China. I traveled in China for a long time in 1932 and saw that transportation was mostly dependent on manpower and animal power, and there were few roads through the fields. However, today there are 47,000 miles of roads. Other buildings, such as railway passes, have also made great progress. As for the municipal administration of Nanjing, its progress is particularly admirable. All of this is enough to make the inland and coastal and river commercial ports have developed transportation and convenient freight. Other aspects, such as irrigation, afforestation, and river management, have also achieved satisfactory results. This is really something we are happy about and is enough to be a prelude to a new era in China. The aviation equipment in China recently and the people's attention to aviation. I have traveled by air many times in China. The most satisfactory one was this Sunday's flight from Beijing to Shanghai, which took less than an hour. Regarding the independence of the Philippines, I want to say something. The Philippines has been under American rule for more than 30 years. Now that the American Congress has allowed it to be autonomous, although its sovereignty still belongs to the United States, all its internal affairs will be returned to the people of the Philippines. The president will also be elected by them. The United States only sends one governor to inspect its administration. In the recent five years, the trade between the United States and the Philippines will remain unchanged except for a few restrictions. However, five years later, until the ten-year trial period before the Philippines is completely independent, the products shipped from the Philippines to the United States must be subject to the treatment of new tariffs. It is found that this matter has a profound impact on the Far East. During this trial period, the people of the Philippines must find new markets to replace the United States and impose a very heavy burden on their industries. We have been invited to visit China and Japan this time, which has made our efforts have the hope of satisfactory results."

Shanghai Minsheng Yarn Factory Closes 130

The Shanghai Minsheng Yarn Factory was founded in 1920, entirely funded and operated by Chinese people. It has more than 1,000 workers and a paid-up capital of 700,000 yuan. It is a joint-stock company. When it was first founded, it had two departments: cotton spinning and wool spinning. The company's authorities, in view of the increasing imports of foreign goods and the loss of money, added weaving machines, dyeing, and finishing machines in 1931 to resist foreign goods and slightly reduce the drain. The products include cotton yarn, wool yarn, woolen cloth, various cotton and wool blankets, etc. The annual production is 9,000 bales of yarn, 40,000 bolts of cloth, 20,000 cotton and wool blankets, and 300,000 military blankets are welcome to be used. Unfortunately, the capital is too small. In recent years, the addition of wool weaving, dyeing, and finishing departments has cost hundreds of thousands of yuan, and the financial tightening has made it difficult to turn around. After a temporary shareholders' meeting, it was resolved to declare liquidation, and lawyers Wu Linkun and accountant Xi Yushu were entrusted to handle the liquidation matters. The company's authorities, in view of the difficult livelihood of the workers and in order to revive national industry, are still trying to raise new funds everywhere, and there is hope of resuming work in a short time.

At this critical moment, we rely on practical relief. If this small loan can be realized as soon as possible, it can still save the desperate situation. If we continue to hesitate and procrastinate, then the overall situation will be lost. The market situation in Shanghai is depressed, and the people are struggling to make a living, which is obvious to all. Among them, the most difficult and difficult thing is the sluggish industrial and commercial business, the expenses are as usual, the commercial goods are piled up like mountains, and the workers are as numerous as the tide. The capital is exhausted on weekdays, and we can still deal with the silver and money industry, but now everyone sweeps the snow in front of their own doors, and the door to business is also interrupted. It is impossible for industry and commerce not to stop their business. Under the continuous closure, Shanghai, the leading commercial port in our country, will never return to its prosperous day. However, in addition to the direct benefit of the silver and money industry, there is no benefit to the ordinary industry and commerce. Therefore, all industries and businesses hope that the small industrial and commercial credit loan initiated by the Banking Association and the Local Association last time will be completed as soon as possible, so as to help them out of their predicament. The matter concerns the overall situation, and it is both important and urgent. We earnestly request that your association work hard to promote its early completion, which is not only the great virtue of a part of industry and commerce, but also all the citizens of Shanghai will benefit from it. Art Exhibition: Preview Day 20 133

Yesterday (the 27th) was the tenth day of the Shanghai preview of the London International Exhibition of Chinese Art. As the closing date approached, visitors purchased tickets to enter and view, making the venue extremely crowded. Moreover, there were visitors from afar, some from Fujian and some from Hubei, who did not hesitate to travel long distances to visit Shanghai, which is sufficient to show the strong interest of Chinese people in art in recent years. Others came from various counties in Jiangsu Province, and there was no day without them. Statistics show that yesterday's visitors numbered nearly three thousand. The news heard yesterday is summarized as follows:

Continued Submission of Antiquities for Display

The Archaeological Group of the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica has continued to send ten selected archaeological examples, as well as two photographs, which were displayed yesterday in the seventh exhibition room of the association. These antiquities are even better than those previously sent by the group, so many visitors stopped in front of the display cases to carefully examine them.

Rubbings of Inscriptions on Anhui Bronzes

The Anhui Provincial Library previously sent four bronze vessels, including a Zu tripod and a Ding cauldron, for display. Two of them each have inscriptions. The inscription on the Ding cauldron reads "Chu King Hui... Temple cast Zhi Ding, Minister Gong... Chang Yi," twelve characters in total. The inscription on the Zhi cauldron reads "One cast, the format is King Gou Liu Nai Wei Zhi," nineteen characters in total. The library has printed rubbings of both and attached explanatory texts, specially submitting them to the association for display and exhibition. The association yesterday (the 27th) replied to the Anhui Provincial Library that it had handled the matter according to the items listed in the letter.

Explanation of Selected Archaeological Examples

Explanations of selected archaeological examples include oracle bones used for divination, oracle bone script, deer head carvings, stone knives, stone axes, and bone tools. Arrowheads, Ge halberds, spears, and axes, and nine other categories have been previously published in this newspaper. We are now publishing the explanations of bronzes, fragments, bronze molds, bone carvings, ivory carvings, and stone carvings to give readers a complete picture. (Ten) Bronze Fragments: With the demise of the Yin Dynasty, the Zhou people looted all of its important vessels. Therefore, no important ritual vessels have been found at the Yin Ruins. However, the selected fragments are sufficient to prove that the bronzes of the Yin people were all cast, and also to prove the variety of types of bronzes that were cast. (Twelve) Bone Carvings, Ivory Carvings, and Stone Carvings: The artifacts of the Yin Ruins that best represent the artistic concepts of the Yin people are bronze molds, bone carvings, ivory carvings, and stone carvings. The bronze molds have been mentioned above. Now, five kinds of bone carvings, ivory carvings, and stone carvings are selected to show their carving and inlay techniques. (End)

Celebrities Visit the Exhibition

Yesterday, the celebrities who visited the exhibition included Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan; Ye Chucang and his wife, Secretary-General of the Central Party Headquarters; Ding Chaowu, a member of the Central Committee; Gu Zhenglun, Commander of the Capital Garrison; and Zou Lin, Vice Minister of Finance. Ye Chucang praised the layout of the exhibition hall, saying that it was remarkable to have achieved such results in a short period of time. Chu Minyi and Gu Zhenglun also visited the exhibition the day before yesterday, and yesterday was their second visit, showing a great interest in art. In addition, many groups came to visit the exhibition. More than 160 students from the Shanghai Municipal Council Girls' School came to visit, making the venue extremely crowded.

Kong Xiangrong Reported to Kong Xiangxi Yesterday on the Progress of the Guantai Closure Project 135

Kong Xiangrong, Standing Committee Member of the National Water Conservancy Commission and Director of the Relief Work Group of the Yellow River Disaster Relief Commission, arrived in Shanghai from Kaifeng the day before yesterday. Yesterday morning at around 8:00 AM, he met with Kong Xiangxi, Chairman of the National Water Conservancy Commission, to report on the progress of the Guantai closure project. Kong Xiangxi stated that the closure project had been completed and had been submitted to the government for inspection and acceptance. He decided to leave Shanghai and return north within one or two days in order to handle the handover. Yesterday, a reporter from the Central News Agency met with Kong Xiangrong, who provided a detailed account of the Guantai closure process, which is recorded as follows:

It is noted that the breach in the Yellow River at Fenglou Shitouzhuang two years ago remained unclosed for several months until the middle of February last year. Kong took over the responsibility on February 15 and the closure was completed within three weeks. This time, the breach in the Huayang Dyke Jiugulu area of Guantai was worked on by the Hebei River Affairs Bureau for five months, but instead, the Guantai breach was scoured to 30 meters, taking away 80% of the river's flow. The central government, recognizing that the situation was escalating and concerned the safety of the three provinces of Hebei, Shandong, and Henan, urgently sought relief measures. If this was not done, a new course would be altered and the locality would be devastated. Kong was ordered to take office at a time of great danger. Fortunately, he was supported by sufficient funds from the central government, transportation assistance from the railway bureau of the Ministry of Railways, and communication assistance from the telegraph bureau of the Ministry of Communications. In addition, the three provincial governments and county governments provided hired boats and carts for procurement, and the people were happy to contribute. Everyone worked diligently as if they were facing a great disaster together, so that the closure was successfully announced in less than two weeks and the flow was stopped in five days, completing the work of cutting off the flow. Incompetent as Kong is, there is nothing to be proud of. He was only attentive and diligent in his duties. However, there are some things that can be recorded: (A) Regarding the procurement and transportation of materials, 1. Ships: More than 400 ships were hired, from Wuzhi in Henan to Lijin in Shandong. It was not easy to gather them on the difficult waterways of the Yellow River. 2. Carts: More than 1,000 carts were hired from the counties near Lanfeng, with funds provided, to transport stones from Lanfeng Station to Chenliukou, opposite Guantai, and then transported by manpower with small carts. 3. Willow branches for brushwood: Each county along the river was responsible for purchasing 10 million catties. From Zheng County to Puyang, special personnel were stationed at the Huayuan, Liushui, ... Liuyuan, Chenqiao, Chenliu, and Lanfeng crossings to collect materials, issue tickets, and receive payments based on the tickets. The group then dispatched ships to transport the materials to the work sites, sailing upstream when the wind was from the north and downstream when the wind was from the south, using the wind direction to increase the speed of transportation within hundreds of miles. 4. Stones: One part was purchased from the Dahu quarry in Xuzhou, Jiangsu, and one part was purchased from the Heshangqiao Xingshan quarry. The Longhai, Pinghan, and Jinpu railways jointly allocated cars and transported them day and night. The North Ning Railway also allocated locomotives to assist. The daily volume of mountain transport gradually increased from hundreds of cubic meters to 1,100 cubic meters. Although the working stones could barely be used, the transportation by car and boat took time. There was no way to meet the needs in terms of mileage. Therefore, boats were used from Gongxian to transport them, and stones were borrowed and purchased from the Henan River Affairs Bureau to assist in the transportation by land and water. This was able to meet the demand. Before and after, 10,000 cubic meters were transported to Lanfeng and Guantai. 5. Lead wire and hemp bags: Both were purchased from Shanghai. One hundred tons of lead wire and 250,000 hemp bags were transported in batches from Shanghai to the construction site. After the closure, there were still 40 tons of lead wire and 50,000 hemp bags being transported to the construction site for storage in case of a major flood. 6. Other ramie, etc., were purchased and transported from Hanzhong and other places to the construction site, reaching 200,000 to 300,000 catties. In addition to those used, the value of the existing materials is more than 100,000 yuan. (B) Regarding the progress of the project, 1. Defensive engineering: At the beginning of the group's management, while concentrating on the collection of various materials, it designed to protect the existing sweeping sections of the east and west dams. The west dam had a draft of more than 10 meters. The east dam had a draft that was deep and sloping inward. Therefore, boulders and hemp bags were thrown to protect the dam feet of all the dams facing the river and behind the river, and willow stone bundles were used to protect the dam feet. The soil compartments between the main and side dams were filled with willow-wrapped soil bags to consolidate the inside and outside of the two dams, so that the mouth of the breach was blocked. 2. Water-permeable willow dam: It was anchored with large willows and pressed into the water, but its power could only slightly divide the flow and could not silt up. It was originally intended to make a substantial water-diverting dam, but due to the need to block the mouth of the breach with stone materials, there was not enough to allocate, so it was not made. Only temporary floating boats were added to make the heavy anchors fall and increase the diversion of the flow. The success of the closure still lies in the willow stone pillows in the form of jujube kernels, which were taken by the construction of the willow stone bundles. 3. Blocking and closing work: First, the existing soil dams of the east and west dams were protected with willow stone pillows to a considerable degree of consolidation. Two boats were placed at the Dragon Gate facing the river and tied to the anchor boats facing the river. The pillows were tied to the anchor boats at the end facing the river and slowly lowered to the bottom with a winch. The work was carried out day and night and was finally successful. The east and west dams, facing the river, behind the river, and at the mouth of the breach, used a total of 1,660 willow stone pillows, each about 4 zhang long and 1.5 chi in diameter, weighing about 6,000 catties. This shows the greatness of the project. 4. Closing work: After the closure was completed, 40,000 earth bags were thrown on the river-facing side of the Dragon Gate to make willow sweeps with alternating willow and earth bags. A total of six batches were pressed, but they could not reach the bottom of the water. Each batch was about 1 zhang long. The volume occupied by the 40,000 hemp earth bags and the six batches of closing willow sweeps, plus the stones thrown on the surface of the water, is enough to prove that the depth of the river-facing pit in front of the Dragon Gate is at least 6 or 7 zhang. It can be known that it is by no means the rumor that the Liu Dam can be successfully padded. According to reports, the rumor that the willow dam was successful in silting up and blocking the breach was reported by Qi Shouan, Director of the Hebei River Affairs Bureau, in the name of the chief of the engineering office. During the tense time of the group's breach closure project, Director Qi asked for leave of absence on the pretext of official business, and claimed that he had to start work on the Huayang Dyke Jiugulu area and could not take care of both. He requested to resign from the concurrent position of chief of the engineering office. The group was forced to submit a request for approval, and on April 6, after his leave expired, the group sent Zhu Chang'an, the section chief of the bureau, to continue to take over the acting position, separately notifying the records. However, until the closure was completed in November, he suddenly came to the job reinstatement to indicate that he had been dismissed on the 13th to report to the group, the group's engineering vote approved, the group believes that personnel who have been approved to resign, still use the group's engineering office in the name of, to report to the various departments, there are overstepping their powers, please strictly prohibit the group, etc., has been notified on record, his report has not taken effect, but the entire Guantai work, all by Rong presided over planning, know the most thoroughly, fear that the outside world will be misunderstood, special notes, You Nan to say, Guantai closure was originally a cut-off work, because after Lou flow, Huayang to the nine shares of the road area, will be the mouth of the breach, you can take soil, easy to block the restoration, the group to grab the closure, day and night, sleepless and rest, because the speed of the closure, one can make the people of the three provinces do not mistake the spring ploughing early to return to their hometowns, two can make the Huayang to the nine shares of the road and the Jin Di, all easy to construction, but after the closure, it has been more than half a month, it has been found that the Huayang to the nine shares of the road area, are now dry, repeatedly by the meeting to allocate funds to urge the river bureau to start work, but unexpectedly Yan delay is not in accordance with, yesterday see the newspaper, and false words of employees leaving Guan, can not start, it is not known that at this time to repair the original embankment, and Guantai has not been closed before, very different, with pure soil work, for the easiest in the project, also imperative, not to mention Real Estate Association Publishes the Process of Negotiating Water Prices 137

For the past four or five years, the public concession's tap water has repeatedly increased in price. Since the conversion from the package water system to the water meter system two years ago, water fees have skyrocketed, and users cannot afford to pay them. The Real Estate Association Kui Yanfang, ... Yaoting, Shen Jixuan, Li Bohan, Li Shuxiong, and others protested, and the Public Concession Bureau organized a water price committee, with Feng Bingnan as chairman, who held a fair position. The water meter fee was calculated with a discount, and the water price was fair, benefiting users. Recently, the association, based on the original agreement to increase the surcharges in 1930, requested that the Public Concession Bureau reconsider the water price, since the silver price has reached two shillings. The correspondence is recorded below:

Letter to the Public Concession Bureau

Letter from the Real Estate Association to the General Office of the Public Concession: Respectfully, the Shanghai Water Company requires landlords of neighborhoods to pay a water meter deposit, which is adding to the difficulties of the real estate industry at a time when the real estate industry is declining. We hereby protest and ask your bureau to negotiate with the company to cancel this provision. The deposit is a guarantee, and its cancellation will have no impact on the company's finances, but it will benefit the real estate industry. Also, the surcharge on tap water that was increased in 1930 should be reviewed, since the silver has reached two shillings. We ask your bureau to consider this matter so that the package water fee will return to 6% of the previous amount. It seems that the discount method set by the company since April 1 last year is not applicable to non-water meter areas that still use the package water fee.

Reply Letter from the Public Concession Bureau

Reply Letter from the Public Concession Bureau to the Real Estate Association: (1) Your letter of March 16 regarding the protest against the Shanghai Water Company's deposit for water meters and the request to reconsider the water surcharge has been submitted to the board of directors for review. (2) Respectfully, your letter of March 16 regarding the protest against the Water Company's collection of water meter deposits and the proposal to revise the 25% surcharge in non-metered areas. Landlords of neighborhood houses may request the Water Company to install sub-meters and sign water contracts with tenants to alleviate the difficulties of landlords. This is a reasonable move, as landlords are not responsible for excessive waste by tenants. However, landlords have never used this provision, except when the number of sub-meters saved exceeds the interest on the water meter deposit. In small houses, the installation of sub-meters is not economical due to the low water fees, and some are even a loss, which must be compensated by all users. Your association's request would only increase this loss and is difficult to implement. As for the second paragraph of the letter, there are no non-water meter areas in the concession.

Shanghai Begins Cholera Vaccination Program May 1st, City Health Bureau Entrusts Vaccination Sub-stations 141

As the weather warms, cholera bacteria easily multiply. The city's cholera prevention work has been prepared by the Municipal Health Bureau and will begin free cholera vaccinations on May 1st. In addition to forming vaccination teams to be sent to various locations, it has also entrusted well-known hospitals in the city as vaccination sub-stations in order to make it widespread. Any citizen who wishes to receive this preventive vaccine can go directly to the Health Offices in the areas of Hu Nan, Jiang Wan, Wu Song, Gao Qiao, etc. under the bureau's administration, as well as the Municipal Shanghai Hospital, Zhabei Clinic, the Municipal Central District Simple Clinic, or various sub-stations for free vaccination. It is reported that the bureau has a mixed cholera-typhoid vaccine, which can prevent both cholera and typhoid fever after vaccination, which can be described as killing two birds with one stone. It is also said that if there is a group of more than thirty people, they can write to the bureau to arrange for personnel to be sent for vaccination regularly. The known vaccination sub-stations are as follows: Southeast Hospital of the Nanshi Military Camp, Xin Pu Yu Tang on Pu Yu West Road, Pingmin Charity Clinic on Da Wang Miao Street, Women and Children's Hospital on Fang Xie Road, West Gate, Nanyang Hospital on Xiao Nan Men, Shui Shen Ge Clinic on Xiao Nan Men Street, Municipal Public Education Center on Wen Miao Road, Taizhou Hospital at the intersection of Xin Qiao Street and Min Guo Road, Pu Shan Hospital at No. 1043 Xin Min Road, Lian Yi West Hospital at the Han Qiao Tu of North Station, Red Cross General Hospital on Haig Road, Red Cross Second Hospital on Cade Road, Xin Zha Road, Red Cross Third Hospital on Wai Ma Road, Shiliupu, Hu Nan Civilian Obstetrics and Gynecology Hospital at No. 707 Zhonghua Road, Da Nan Men, Labor Hospital on Xiao Sha Du Road, Tong De Hospital at No. 1, Lane 67, Tong Fu Road, Sino-German Hospital on Fu Xi Road, Shanghai Epidemic Hospital opposite the Great World on Tibet Road, Emergency Epidemic Hospital on North Tibet Road, Hu Xi Commune on Robert Road, Pudong Hospital on Lan Ni Du, Children's Charity Clinic on Wu Zhen Road.

Rice Prices Soar Daily, Tianjin and Hebei Suffer Wind Disaster, Inland Demand High, Authorities Studying Remedial Measures 142

Since last year, our country has been affected by drought, resulting in poor harvests. Rice merchants in this city have ordered foreign rice from foreign merchants to regulate the market. More than four million bags of foreign rice have arrived in port one after another, of which about three million bags have been sold. About one million bags will arrive soon. However, recently the inland demand for rice is very strong. According to last month, more than 1.1 million bags were sold. Now, the total of those arriving and those in stock is only more than 2 million bags. However, the new grain will not be available until a few months later, and the foreign rice can only last for more than two months. Therefore, although it was at the end of April a month ago, the price of rice not only did not decrease, but also increased. Now, the area of Tianjin and Hebei has suddenly suffered the impact of wind disasters, and food prices have soared. Most grain merchants hoard and hoard, unwilling to sell, so the price of rice will inevitably rise, causing panic among the people for food. The authorities will also study remedial measures.

Wei Tingrong Case, Two Kidnappers Withdraw Appeal, After Judge Explains Original Judgment, Two Bandits Suddenly Realize and Request Withdrawal of Appeal 143

On July 24, 1929, in the case of the kidnapping of Wei Tingrong, former commander of the French Concession Volunteer Corps and Chinese director of the French Municipal Council, the French-Chinese Bank, and the owner of the Yuan Tai Foreign Goods Company, the French police arrested the bandit gang members Zhu Jingcheng (also known as Xiangfeng, 37 years old this year, from Huaining, Anhui, former member of the Anhui Finance Department), Chen Zhongheng (also known as Wang Kui, 35 years old, from Wenzhou, Zhejiang, former pharmacist), and Tang Shiliang (36 years old, from Songjiang). The three were interrogated and sentenced by the former French Public Concession to five years of imprisonment, and after the expiration of the term, they were sent to the inland government for interrogation. The three prisoners were detained until February of this year, when the five-year term expired. The Second Special District Prison transferred the three prisoners to the Second Special Court, requesting a review. After Judge Qiu Huan-ying conducted the final interrogation, he sentenced Zhu Jingcheng to seven years of imprisonment for instigating kidnapping for ransom, and Chen Zhongheng and Tang Shiliang to six years of imprisonment each for helping kidnapping for ransom. The number of days of detention before the judgment was determined to be one day of imprisonment for every two days, and the number of days in prison was considered as execution. Unexpectedly, after the verdict was announced, Zhu insulted the judge in court for unfair judgment. After Judge Qiu reported the information to the president, Zhu was transferred to the procuratorate for interrogation and ordered to be returned to custody pending investigation. The details have been reported in the newspapers. Now, after receiving the judgment, the three prisoners detained in the detention center, except for Tang Shiliang, who gave up the appeal and has been sent to prison to continue serving his sentence, Zhu and Chen expressed their dissatisfaction with the review judgment and hired lawyers Zhang Shizhao and Peng Yuanxun to file an appeal to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. With the approval of the Third Branch of the High Court, the presiding judge Guo Dezhang, together with Judges Xiong Ping and Wang Cheng, and Prosecutor Zhang Zongru, specially opened a full deliberation court for interrogation. They also summoned the victim Wei Tingrong and the accomplices Tang Shiliang and Cai Weicai, who were executing their sentences in prison, to testify. Lawyer Yao Zhaodi represented the police department in court. After the court opened, the appellants Zhu Jingcheng and Chen Zhongheng were brought to the court. First, they were asked about their age, address, and occupation. Then, they were ordered to state the reasons for their appeal against the judgment. According to Zhu, the reasons for the people's appeal are very sufficient, but now they are unwilling to appeal and request permission to withdraw the appeal in court, preferring to suffer in prison for another two years. When asked about Chen, he said that he was very confused and unclear about the current judgment. The judgment stated that the principal offender was only sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. I am an accomplice and have already had my sentence reduced by one-half. Why am I still sentenced to imprisonment? On this point, I request the court to explain. Judge Guo verified the confession and explained to Chen that according to the law on punishing bandits in kidnapping cases, he should be sentenced to death. According to the amnesty regulations, the sentence is reduced by one-half, and he should be sentenced to life imprisonment. After further investigation, you are an accomplice, and the sentence is reduced by another two-thirds. The criminal law stipulates that you should be sentenced to six to twelve years of imprisonment. The original trial was based on these points and reduced the sentence repeatedly, only sentencing you to six years of imprisonment. If you think the six-year sentence is too heavy, you can appeal now, but whether the original trial's sentencing is light or heavy can only be clarified after the trial. There is no way to know whether your sentence is light or heavy now. Chen listened and said that after the court's explanation, he understood and was unwilling to appeal, requesting permission to withdraw the appeal. The official then said to the two prisoners that now that you want to withdraw the appeal, the original sentence will be final and you will not be able to appeal again in the future. You should consider it carefully. The two prisoners said that they would not appeal again. At this point, the court ordered the witnesses Tang Shiliang and Cai Weicai to be brought to the court and informed them that today they were being brought in for interrogation because of the appeal case of Zhu Jingcheng and Chen Zhongheng. Now that Zhu and Chen have withdrawn their appeals, there is no need to interrogate you any further. After the announcement, Zhu and Chen were ordered to be returned to the detention center to wait to be sent to prison for execution. Cai and Tang were sent back to prison. Wei Tingrong was summoned to the court and informed that the purpose of summoning you today was to ask you about what happened at that time. Because Zhu and Chen have returned to appeal, there is no need to ask you any further. You can go back. Wei listened and retreated, and the court adjourned.

The ferries at various wharves along the beach in the Nanshi area of this city, such as the Shiliupu Pier and the Baitou South Pier, have been successively converted into ferries and towed by small ferries, which is convenient for travel and greatly benefits the public. The number of people traveling to and from Pudong and Puxi is very large and never interrupted. After giving the bank draft and receiving the money, they fled in a hurry. The defendant was at the scene, holding a pistol, etc. (2) At 7:00 am on November 19 last year, the robbery of the Ye Rongjun military uniform shop at No. 20, Lane 171, Yuanfang Road failed. The defendant and Ye fought each other, and the copper basin and felt hat fell off. He shot and seriously injured him, killing him. After the case occurred, the military uniform shop closed down, and his wife, Mrs. Dai, and shop assistants all returned home, so they could not be summoned. The defendant admitted to shooting and performing at the scene in the police station. At that time, a felt hat of the defendant was seized and presented for inspection. Lu confessed that what he said in the police station was untrue. Because I committed many robberies, I was sentenced to a long-term imprisonment. I heard that robbers in prison cannot eat enough and suffer all kinds of pain. It is better to admit it and be shot early to avoid suffering piecemeal. I tried to commit suicide several times in the police station, but could not get my wish, so I admitted it directly. In fact, I did not hear about this case (3) At 1:00 pm on December 15 last year, he colluded with the second defendant Yang Cheng to rob the Zhang Zhiqing iron factory at No. 18, Lane 355, Broadway, of silver dollars and clothes. They still felt it was too little and forced him to hand over a large amount of property with a gun. The victim Zhang was afraid of being harmed and gave a Shanghai Commercial Bank draft of 700 yuan. After a fellow member was sent to collect it, he also replied by telegram and left. Yang also recognized that Zhang had invited him to get the money and was on par with Lu. Lu Ahui fired a shot to show his power, and I also fired a shot into the sky and fled out the door. The Si Ge Yu Chunjin testified that Lu had fired at me to harm my life. Abandoning a Dying Adopted Daughter-in-Law, Origin of the Female Corpse on Jufu Road, Wang Libao and Others Detained Pending Investigation 151

A nameless female corpse, about thirteen or fourteen years old, was found abandoned on wasteland opposite No. 160 at the intersection of Route des Soeurs and Rue Amiral Courbet, French Concession, at 10:00 am on the 23rd of this month. The French police reported the incident and sent detectives to transport the body to the autopsy office. They reported to the Second Special District Court, which commissioned Prosecutor Wang Ren to conduct an autopsy with the forensic doctor and found that the deceased had died from measles symptoms during her lifetime. Because no family members could be found, he ordered Tongren Shop Yuantang to hand over the body for photos and burial on behalf of the family. On the one hand, the French police sent detectives to investigate and arrest the corpse-throwing criminal to be brought to justice for interrogation. Before her death, Wang carried the girl out and abandoned her. She lived for two days, which was inconvenient. On the 21st, I rented the back building of No. 607. At 4:30 am on the 23rd, the illness became more serious. I intended to send her to the hospital, but when I reached the intersection of Jufu Road, the girl's illness worsened and she fainted, so I threw her down, etc. The police chief ordered them to be detained and sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court yesterday. According to the police lawyer Gu Shouxi's statement of the case, the defendant and others were arrested for abandoning a person to death. The police station still needs to investigate and requested a postponement. They will file a lawsuit after the investigation is completed. After reviewing the report, Baishi Li Changnian briefly questioned the defendants and ordered them to postpone the hearing until May 2. The defendants were returned to custody.

Since the beginning of spring, the weather in this city has been very cold and the weather has been unstable. From the 25th (Thursday), it suddenly turned warm, and the temperature on the Fahrenheit thermometer rose above 80 degrees. People on the road who were wearing lined clothes felt warm and easily changed into single clothes. The room was also very stuffy, quite like the atmosphere of early summer.

The International Settlement Volunteer Corps: Grand Review Yesterday; 2,600 Members from Various Countries Participated; Inspected by British Commander Major General Seckle 153

The annual grand review of the International Settlement Volunteer Corps was held at the racecourse yesterday at 3:10 PM. The reviewing stand was set up in front of the Race Club. A total of approximately 2,600 people participated. The details are recorded as follows:

Participating Units: The grand review was divided into two columns. The first column was led by the Headquarters, followed by the Cavalry, the Signal Corps, the 1st Battalion of Infantry (including Battalion Headquarters, A Company, B Company, Scottish Company, Jewish Company, Anti-Aircraft Platoon), the 2nd Battalion of Infantry (including Battalion Headquarters, American Company, Portuguese Company, Filipino Company, American Machine Gun Platoon), the 3rd Battalion of Infantry (including Battalion Headquarters, 1st Company, 2nd Company, 3rd Company, 4th Company), and the Composite Battalion (including armored car squadron members, Japanese Company, Chinese Company, Translator Company, and Transport Corps members). The second column consisted of armored cars, artillery, light artillery and mortar units, engineer units, and transport units. A total of five mobile kitchen vehicles were present. There were 2,600 corps members from various countries in total.

Forming and Departure: Yesterday at 2:00 PM sharp, the corps members from various countries, following the order of Commander Gleean, assembled at the racecourse. An order was issued to all corps members stating that the grand review was a most important ceremony to demonstrate competence, and those who were absent without reason could not be considered competent. Uniforms were to be neat, and attention should be paid to military bearing in addition to the various procedures. At 3:25 PM, general mobilization began. Each unit departed from the north gate of the racecourse on Jing'an Temple Road. Jing'an Temple Road, from Tibet Road to Tongfu Road, was temporarily closed to traffic from 3:15 PM onwards. The police department dispatched Chinese and Western mounted police, car patrol, and plainclothes detectives to maintain order. Onlookers lining the streets were extremely crowded. After departure, the units proceeded along Jing'an Temple Road, passed the reviewing stand in front of the Race Club, turned onto Xiejiao Road heading south, then onto Tongfu Road heading east, and then onto Weihaiwei Road, then heading north on Mahe Road and entering the racecourse.

Conducting the Review: A temporary reviewing stand made of wood was erected in the open space in front of the Race Club, and three special guest seating areas were set up. One, the "　" section, was for members of the Police Committee and their wives. One, the "K" section, was for officers and their wives, and civil officials from the diplomatic missions and organizations. One, the "L" section, was for domestic officials and their wives, and other invited guests. The reviewing officers were Major General Seckle, the British military commander in China, and Colonel Gleean, the commander of the International Settlement Volunteer Corps. The Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Council, Arnold, also joined in the review. The corps members passing the reviewing stand saluted the reviewing officers, and the British military band played music. The first column was mostly composed of the Chinese Company infantry, led by Commander Chen Shixia of the Chinese Company. The second column included ten armored cars, eight artillery vehicles, seven engineer vehicles, four transport vehicles, and five mobile kitchen vehicles.

Welcoming Guests: Yesterday's spectators included American Consul General Edwin S. Cunningham, British Consul General Pelly, Japanese Consul General Ishii, Shanghai Municipal Police Commissioner Cai Jingjun, and military officers and their wives, civil officials, etc., from various countries stationed in Shanghai, as well as Chinese and foreign people standing on the roadside to watch. The total was about 50,000 people. As for the mobile kitchen vehicles, each vehicle was equipped with stoves and all necessary equipment, and staffed with two Chinese cooks. It was heard that this was established by Commander Gleean. This time it was just a test. If suitable, the problem of meals for the Volunteer Corps mobilization in the future can be resolved.

Commander's Encouragement: After the International Settlement Volunteer Corps entered the racecourse at 4:00 PM, traffic on Jing'an Temple Road was restored to its original state. Commander Colonel Gleean then gave a speech, which translated as: Today, the International Settlement Volunteer Corps held its annual grand review. The number of participating corps members was very large, unprecedented. The spirit was very good, the uniforms were neat, and the military bearing was full of vigor during the salutes. This commander is very happy and congratulates all corps members for their efforts. The corps then disbanded.

Shanghai Literacy Education Committee Promotes Literacy Education Propaganda Outline 159

(1) Propaganda Goals

(1) Explain the pain of illiteracy and the convenience of literacy, as well as its relationship to the country and society, so that the public knows the importance of literacy education, rises up to support the work of this committee, literate people are willing to bear the responsibility of persuasion, publicity, or teaching people to read, and illiterate people are willing to receive literacy education and enter the literacy schools run by this committee.

(2) Make the public aware that the literacy education movement promoted by this committee is not just a simple literacy education, but a patriotic movement that combines literacy education, common sense guidance, and civic training, so the public must enthusiastically support and actively participate.

(3) Make the public aware that the current methods of literacy are divided into two types: one is remedial education in school, and the other is remedial education outside of school. Under the first method, this committee has decided to establish 220 literacy schools starting from July 1st, with a total of 1,320 classes (postponed in the concessions), forcing illiterate people to attend school in batches for one hour each day, for a period of two months. Under the second method, this committee has requested that the Shanghai Party and government organs stipulate by order that all Party members and school students have the obligation to teach people to read. Illiterate people who have real difficulties and cannot attend school are allowed to find their own teachers or be introduced by this food to be filled by the above personnel, receive textbooks, and study at home, waiting for this committee to convene a test after a certain period of time. If the test passes, this committee can also award a graduation certificate.

(4) Make the public aware that handling this literacy education must start with investigation. Therefore, this committee will dispatch a large number of investigators to investigate illiterate people door-to-door between May and June, so as to teach students according to their aptitude in the future. However, door-to-door investigation is quite difficult, and we hope that the public will assist and facilitate it, and must not make things difficult or misunderstand. If you are willing to widely publicize and persuade verbally, this committee will feel greatly benefited.

(5) Create a warm and strong reading atmosphere, at least make the public aware that this city will force all illiterate people to receive literacy education starting from July 1st this year. If there are illiterate people who do not know how to cherish themselves and are unwilling to learn characters, this committee will impose a fine or labor service as punishment, and after one year the Qing Municipal Government will deport them.

(2) The Significance of Literacy Education

The significance of literacy education is very important. The following is a summary of the main points: (1) Regarding the individual: The average number of illiterate people in our country is more than 80%. These people cannot write letters, cannot keep accounts, cannot read newspapers, do not know the postings on the walls, do not understand the announcements of the official offices, and do not understand the general trend of the world. Having eyes is equal to having no eyes, and the pain is truly unbearable.

(2) Regarding society: The element of social evolution is knowledge, and the bridge to obtain knowledge is writing. Therefore, if you want to spread knowledge, you must first teach writing, and if you want to obtain knowledge, you must first know writing. Therefore, if you want society to progress, everyone must be literate.

(3) Regarding the people: Our national rights are becoming increasingly low, and the national crisis is serious. If we want to revive the nation, we must first awaken national consciousness and inspire national spirit, and the way to start is literacy education. 100% of the people in Germany are literate, so their national power can gradually become stronger. If more than 80% of the people in our country are still illiterate in the future, it will be difficult to resolve the national crisis and it will be difficult to revive the nation.

(4) Regarding civil rights: People today like to talk about democratic politics, thinking that Chinese politics should be managed by the people themselves. This theory is very attractive, and the current government does not oppose it. However, most people today are illiterate, and cannot even write their own names. How can the government hand over political power to the people? Therefore, if the people want to expand their own civil rights, they must work hard to promote literacy education. In the past, autocratic governments, in order to deceive the people, implemented policies of ignorance and did not allow the people to be educated. Now, the municipal government, for the purpose of benefiting the people, is promoting literacy education on a large scale, and the people must not miss this great opportunity.

(5) Regarding people's livelihood: Our people's livelihood is declining due to backward production, and the reason for backward production is the lack of development of science. If we want to solve the people's livelihood problem in the future, then all industries, agriculture, commerce, transportation, etc. must use scientific methods to actively improve. The principle of "saving the country through science" has been recognized by everyone, but if people are not literate, how can scientific knowledge be instilled? Therefore, if you want to solve the people's livelihood problem (the problem of food, clothing, housing, and transportation), you must first promote literacy education.

As mentioned above, literacy education is the foundation of all education, and it is necessary to actively promote it for the country and the people. Moreover, the literacy education that this city intends to promote is not just simple literacy education. In addition to literacy education, there is also common sense guidance and civic training, so its significance is even more important.

(3) Public Enrollment and Remedial Education Methods

Illiterate people enroll in school for remedial education. This is one of the literacy education methods in this city. The main points are recorded as follows:

(1) This city will implement compulsory literacy education starting from July 1, 1935. All illiterate people in this city should receive literacy education.

(2) This city will implement compulsory literacy education for a period of one year, from July 1, 1935 to June 30, 1936.

(3) The class time of literacy schools should be selected by each out-of-school person at the time of the survey within the specified time (approximately children and women during the day, and adult men in the evening) from three to six types, and the literacy schools will coordinate and designate them. Household workers and shop employees should be given convenience by their employers to attend classes, and should not be arbitrarily made difficult.

(4) People who should receive literacy education, if they delay enrollment without reason after receiving the admission notice from the literacy school, in addition to being forced to enroll, will also be fined between two dimes and five yuan, or be ordered to perform labor service for more than two hours and less than five days. The same applies to those who are absent from class without reason. Those who have a reason to ask for leave in the middle and are approved by the literacy school must make up the lesson within the specified time. For the penalties in the preceding paragraph, adult men and women will be fined themselves, and minors will be fined their parents.

(5) The penalties in Article 4 will be decided by the district office after being reported by each literacy school, and the Public Security Bureau will be notified to carry out the penalties, and will be reported to the City Literacy Education Committee for the record on a monthly basis.

(6) Literacy schools do not charge any fees to their students, and textbooks are also provided by the school. However, other school supplies, such as pencils and paper, should be prepared by the students themselves.

(7) Students of literacy schools who pass the examination after the teaching period expires will be issued an initial general education certificate by the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee.

(8) People who should receive literacy education, if they cannot attend classes due to an accident, should explain the reason to the district office or to the nearby literacy school and report it to the district office. After the district office verifies the facts, they may be allowed to study on their own outside the school. Separate measures will be formulated for the aforementioned out-of-school remedial education.

(4) Public Off-Campus Tutoring Measures

Illiterate people can have off-campus tutoring. This is the second method of literacy education in this city. The main points are recorded as follows:

(1) Illiterate people, if they have real difficulties and cannot study at a literacy school, should follow these measures and the articles of association of the Literacy Education Service Corps for off-campus tutoring.

(2) Illiterate people who have off-campus tutoring should report to the district office of the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee or the nearby literacy school before tutoring, and report to the district office. Only after the district office verifies that there are indeed difficulties and approves it can they start.

(3) People who have off-campus tutoring must follow the articles of association of the Literacy Education Service Corps and designate a teacher. Before starting tutoring, they must fill out two copies of the volunteer form.

(4) The time for off-campus tutoring is determined by the person and their teacher, but after the time is determined, teaching must be carried out on time.

(5) People who have off-campus tutoring must collect literacy textbooks from the district office. No fees will be charged.

(6) In addition to literacy education, people who have off-campus tutoring may be given civic training and common sense guidance by the district office or the service corps branch, and must not evade it.

(7) People who have off-campus tutoring must be tested once or twice a month and must not evade it.

(8) People who have off-campus tutoring should be examined by the service corps branch or the district office after a considerable period of time (approximately two or three months) and after reading all the literacy textbooks. Those who pass the examination will be given an initial general education certificate.

(9) People who have off-campus tutoring and whose performance is too poor may be ordered by the district office to restudy at a nearby literacy school.

(5) Charter of the Literacy Education Service Corps

The Literacy Education Service Corps mentioned above is a supplement to literacy schools. Its charter has been formulated. The main points are recorded below:

(1) The Shanghai Literacy Education Service Corps (hereinafter referred to as the Corps) aims to contribute its abilities, serve the people, and assist the government in promoting literacy education.

(2) Teachers and students of all levels of schools and private schools in this city who agree with the purpose of this Corps and are willing to accept the supervision and guidance of the Corps may register with the branch of this Corps and become members after being approved by the head of the branch.

(3) This Corps has a general Corps in the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee and branches in schools and private schools at all levels. The branches are named Shanghai Literacy Education Service Corps ×× School (Private School) Branch.

(4) This Corps has one Corps leader and one Corps deputy leader, who are filled by the chairman and vice chairman of the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee. There is also one general secretary and two deputy general secretaries, who are appointed by the Qihai Literacy Education Committee.

(5) Each branch has one head, who is filled by the school principal or private school teacher where the branch is located, and may have several deputy heads, who are filled by teachers at all levels. The above-mentioned head is appointed by the head of this Corps, and the deputy heads are appointed by the head of this Corps upon the recommendation of the head of each branch.

(6) All members of this Corps have the responsibility to teach people to read. Each member must find at least two illiterate people (including children) in each period (two months) to teach them to read. The teaching time is determined by the teacher and the students, but teaching must be carried out on time after the time is determined.

(7) When teaching begins, members should, together with the people they are teaching, fill out two copies of the volunteer form in accordance with the format set by the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee. One copy is kept by the branch, and one copy is sent by the branch to the district office of the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee for the record.

(8) Members should fill out two copies of the teaching status each month according to the forms made by this Corps, one kept by the branch and one submitted to this Corps for evaluation.

(9) When a member has finished teaching, they should immediately report to the head of the branch and notify the students to go to the head of the branch for testing on a regular basis. If the test passes, the head of the branch will notify the district office of the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee to issue an initial general education certificate, but the district office may re-examine. If it is deemed unqualified, the original member should teach again. Those whose performance is too poor may be directly sent by the district office to a literacy school for compulsory education.

(10) During the teaching process of members, the head or deputy head of the branch should test the students at least once a month. This Corps and the district office of the Shanghai Literacy Education Committee may also send people to conduct spot checks at any time.

(11) The head of the branch should gather all the people taught by the members of the branch at least every two weeks or in batches to conduct civic training and common sense guidance. The method will be formulated separately.

(12) If the branch is a middle or higher school, and its members find it inconvenient to leave the school to individually teach illiterate people, they may set up a people's school or literacy school to replace it. The examination of the grades of the aforementioned schools is subject to the provisions of the above articles.

(13) If the number of members of the branch exceeds one-quarter of the number of students in the school, and more than three-quarters of the members have taught people in each of the three periods, this Corps will give a certificate of merit at the end of the third period. If the number exceeds one-half, and all the members have taught people in the three periods, this Corps will award a banner in addition to asking the Shanghai Education Bureau to issue an order to commend the principal.

(14) If the number of members of the branch cannot exceed one-fifth of the number of students in the school, or the number of people taught by the members is less than one-half on average in each of the three periods, this Corps will ask the Shanghai Education Bureau to reprimand the principal according to the circumstances.

(15) If a member teaches literacy to more than three people in one period and all have passed the test and obtained certificates, the head of the branch will give a certificate of merit. Those who exceed ten people will also be awarded a banner by this Corps to encourage them. Those who do not work hard will be warned by the head of the branch, or have their membership revoked, or have their civil score deducted.

(16) For branches that set up schools in accordance with Article 14 (i.e., Article 12 above), the number of people taught by their members is offset by the number of people taught.

(6) Propaganda Slogans

(1) Having eyes but not knowing characters is like being half-blind.

(2) Just because you don't know characters, you have suffered all the hardships.

(3) Using both hands and brains is a great thing for old people.

(4) The content of literacy education: (1) Literacy education, (2) Common sense guidance, (3) Civic training.

(5) Literacy education is a patriotic movement with unexpected effects.

(6) Literate people have the responsibility to teach illiterate people.

(7) Employers should give their workers the opportunity to become literate.

(8) Teaching people to read is better than building a seven-story pagoda.

(9) Literacy schools will be set up nearby, with no tuition fees and free books. Illiterate people should spend an hour each day to study and can graduate in two months.

(10) If illiterate people refuse to learn to read, the municipal government will impose a fine or labor service, and may even deport them in the future.

Special Publication

Bank of Communications Business Report (II) 160

A. Differences in the International Economy

Since the abandonment of the gold standard by the United Kingdom, Japan, and the United States, most countries have adopted methods such as reducing currency value and exchange rates, and industrial control and tariff barriers, as prerequisites for restoring their national economies. This year's economic policies continue to be implemented and are becoming more stringent. For countries that have abandoned the gold standard, the production prices and export trade of the United Kingdom and the United States have generally increased, the number of unemployed people has decreased, the cost of living index for the people has not changed dramatically, and the purchasing power is better than before. Japan's progress is particularly significant. As for countries that maintain the gold standard, with the exception of Germany's new economic policy, which is different, countries such as France have not failed to use control methods to seek self-defense, but the domestic currency value has not fallen sharply, and the external exchange rate has risen, so production has decreased, prices have fallen, unemployment has increased, and exports have declined, which is the opposite of countries that have abandoned the gold standard. Although the international situation is not entirely the same, it is in the same position for our country's front. All trade markets regard our country as the tail end. This can be asserted. As for the silver issue, it is even more serious. The United States implemented the Silver Act in June, purchasing 1.3 billion ounces of silver, and announced the nationalization of silver in August. Silver from all over the world rushed to the United States like a torrent. According to a survey by Handy & Harman, an American company, the world's silver production this year totaled 181.2 million ounces. The supply from all parties totaled 255 million ounces, of which China sold as much as 200 million ounces, exceeding the world's output and accounting for approximately four-fifths of the world's supply. Silver is the lifeblood of the financial system of silver standard countries. The amount of outflow is so large that the impact of international economic policies on our country's economic undertakings directly affects financial undertakings. (To be continued)

In Search of Zhang Zhifu 161

Zhang Luwen, styled Zhifu, a native of Nanjing, currently about 50 years old, of medium build, with a round face, fair complexion, and short beard, wearing a green wool robe and a black satin jacket, due to a nervous breakdown after an illness, suddenly left his Beijing residence at around 6:00 PM on the 19th of this month and has since disappeared. His family has been searching everywhere, but his whereabouts are unknown. The whole family is deeply worried, and his wife has fallen ill, with the children surrounding her, weeping and wailing miserably, a heartbreaking scene to witness. If any kind-hearted person finds him, please send him back to the Zhang residence at No. 2, Huiwen Lane, North Gate Bridge, Nanjing, or contact Mr. Zhang Xi-wu at this newspaper, so that the family can be reunited. They will be handsomely rewarded.

Hua Hua Silk and Satin Company: Grand Sale Starting May 1st - Clearing Stock Due to Landlord Taking Back Property - Unbeatable Bargains Cheaper Than Any Competitor 167

Hua Hua Silk and Satin Company, located on Third Ma Road (三馬路) and Shi Road (石路), has been in business for many years and rents the building of the Silk Industry Building. Now, because the landlord, the Silk Industry Bank, wants to expand its business and add a trust department, it wants to take back the property for its own use. The company has begun to sort out all the silk and satin in stock, and after the sorting is completed, all the stock will be sold off at extremely low prices starting from May 1st, regardless of cost, with the aim of clearing everything out. According to employees of the company, this sale includes all kinds of fashionable goods that are priced below cost, unlike other stores that only use one or two cheap items as bait to attract customers. Therefore, the prices are so low that no competitor can match them. It is expected that customers will be extremely crowded. It can be seen that the company's sale is a great sacrifice.

The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait are turning cloudy from cloudy, with fog, and the wind is gentle and unstable. The weather east of North Luzon is bad, due to a hurricane moving north or northeast. The center of the hurricane was at noon yesterday about 120 miles within 14 degrees north latitude and 129 degrees east longitude. The wind force is unknown.
